        <body>
            <div n="4" type="sthāna">

                <div n="21" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 21]</head>





                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ śūkadoṣacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vilikhya sarṣapīṃ samyak kaṣāyair avacūrṇṇayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyeṣv eva kurvīta tailañ ca vraṇaropaṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭhīlikāṃ jalaukābhir grāhayed bahuśo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā cānupaśāmyantīṃ kaphagranthivad uddharet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedayed grathitāṃ śaśvan nāḍīṃ svedena buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhoṣṇair upanāhaiś ca susvinnair upanāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kumbhīkāṃ pākam āpannāṃ cchindyāc chodhya ca ropayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tailena lodhratriphalātindukāmrakṛtena vā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jalāyukābhir alajīṅ grāhayet svedayīta ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyais teṣu siddhañ ca tailaṃ ropaṇam iṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balātailena siddhena mṛditam pariṣecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥ snigdhaiś ca madhuraiḥ sukhoṣṇair upanāhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sammūḍhapiṭakāṃ kṣipraṃ jalaukābhir upācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhitvā paryāgataṃ cāpi lepayen madhusarpiṣā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avamanthe gate pākaṃ bhinne tailaṃ vidhīyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhavājakarṇṇāśvakarṇṇasallakīkvāthasādhitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyām puṣkarikāyāṃ tu śītāṃ sarvāṃ prayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sparśahāryāṃ hared raktaṃ madhuraiḥ pradihed api |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrekṣurasasarpirbhiḥ secayec ca suśītalaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uttamākhyāṃ tu piṭakāṃ baḍisenoddhared bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         uddhṛtya madhusaṃyuktaiḥ kaṣāyair avacūrṇṇayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakriyā vidhātavyā likhite śatapośanake |
                        <caesura/>
                         pṛthak parṇyādisiddhañ ca deyan tailam anantaraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāṃ prayuñjyāt kuśalaṃ tvakpākasya visarpavat ||
                        <caesura/>
                         raktavidradhivac cāpi kriyāṃ śoṇitaje rbude | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyakalkasarpīṃṣi tailacūrṇṇarasakriyāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhane ropaṇe caiva vīkṣya vīkṣyāvacārayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hitañ ca sarpiṣaḥ pānaṃ pathyañ cāpi virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hitaḥ śoṇitamokṣaś ca yac cāpi laghu bhojanaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.21.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.21.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arbudam māṃsapākañ ca vidradhiṃ tilakālakaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyākhyāya hi kurvīta bhiṣak teṣām pratikriyām iti || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer"> cicikitsāsthāne 21 || || 0 ||</p>



                </div>

                <div n="22" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 22]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto mukharogāṇāṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvidhena snehena madhucchiṣṭayutena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vātikebhyañjanakaṃ kāryaṃnāḍīsvedam tathāpi ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         oṣṭhaprakope bhiṣajā sālvaṇaṃ copanāhanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mastiṣke caiva nasye ca tailaṃ vātaharai sritaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śrīveṣṭakaṃ sarjarasaṃ gugguluṃ suradāru ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭīmadhukacūrṇṇañ ca hitamatra pralepane |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaraktābhighātotthaṃ jalokābhir upācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittavidradhivac cāpi kriyāṃ kuryād aśeṣataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanaṃ dhūmaṃ svedaṃ kavaḍadhāraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtaraktaprayoktavyam oṣṭhakope kaphātmake |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         trikaṭuṃ svarjikākṣāraṃ kṣārañ ca yavaśūkajaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudrayuktaṃ vidhātavyam etac ca pratisāraṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         medoje svedite bhinne śodhite jvalano hitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṃgulodhratriphalā sakṣaudraṃ pratisāraṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etad oṣṭhaprakopānāṃ sādhyānāṃ karma kīrttitaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dantamūlagatānāṃ tu rogāṇāṃ karma ucyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītāde hṛtaraktasya toyanāgarasarṣapān ||
                        <caesura/>
                         niḥkvāthya triphalāñ cāpi kuryād gaṇḍūṣadhāraṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         priyaṅgavaś ca mustā ca triphalā ca pralepanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyañ ca siddhaṃ triphalāmadhukotpalapadmakaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dantapuppuṭake kāryaṃ taruṇe raktamokṣaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa pañcalavaṇaṃ kṣāraṃ sakṣaudraṃ pratisāraṇaṃ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirekaś ca hito nasyaṃ snigdhaś ca bhojanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         visrāvite dantaveṣṭe vraṇāṃ tu pratisārayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lodhrapatraṅgamadhukalakṣācūrṇṇairmadhūttaraiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gaṇḍūṣe kṣīriṇo yojyāḥ sakṣaudraghṛtaśarkarāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kākolyādau daśakṣīrasiddhaṃ sarpiś ca nastataḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sauṣirehṛtarakte tu lodhramustarasāñjanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.17"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīre daśaguṇā sarpiḥ siddhaṃ nasye ca pūjitaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kriyāṃ paridare kuryāt śītādoktaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśodhyobhayata kāryaṃ śiraścopakuśe hitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kākodamvarikāgojīpatrair visrāvayed asṛk |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudrayuktaiḥ salavaṇaiḥ savyoṣaiḥ pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalyaḥ sarṣapā śvetāḥ nāgaraṃ naiculaṃ phalaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhodakena saṃsṛjya kavaḍantasya yojayet ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛtaṃ madhurakaiḥ siddhaṃ hitaṃ kavaḍanasyayoḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śastreṇa dantavaidarbhadantamūlāni śodhayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥkṣāraṃ prayuñjīta kriyāḥ sarvāś ca śītalāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uddhṛtyādhikamāṃsan tu tato gnim avacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         krimidantakavac cātra vidhiḥ kāryo vijānatā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cchitvād himāṃsaṃ sakṣaudrairimaiś cūrṇṇaiḥ samācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         vacātejavatīpāṭhāsvarjikāyāvaśūkajaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣaudradvitīyā pippalyaḥ kavaḍaś cātrakīrttitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paṭolanimvatriphalākaṣāyāś cātra dhāvanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siro virekaś ca hito dhūmovairecanaś ca yaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.26ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmānyaṃ karma nāḍīnāṃ viśeṣaṃ cātra me śruṇu ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.26cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yaddantamadhijāyeta nāḍīdantaṃ tamuddharet |
                        <caesura/>
                         chitvā māṃsāni śastreṇa yadi noparijo bhavet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhayitvā dahec cāpi kṣāreṇa jvalanena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upekṣite tu daśane gatirhanvasthi dārayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt samūlaṃ daśanam uddhared bhagnamasthi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         uddhṛte tūttare dante śoṇitaṃ saṃprasicyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.30ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         raktātiyogāt pūrvoktā rogā ghorā bhavanti ca |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.30cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.31ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         calam apy uttaman dantam ato nāpahared bhiṣak |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.31cd"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyajātīmadanakaṭukasvādukaṇṭakaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lodhramañjiṣṭhakhadirayaṣṭyāhvaiś cāpi yat kṛtaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ saṃśodhane taddhihanyād dantigatāṃ gatiṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kīrttitā dantamūleṣu kriyā danteṣu vakṣyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhoṣṇaḥ snehakavaḍāḥ sarpiṣastrivṛtasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         niryūhaś cānilaghnānāṃ dantaharṣapramardanāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snaihikaś ca hito dhūmo nasyaṃ snaihikam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasā rasai yavāgvaś ca kṣīrasantānika ghṛtaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36ab"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.36cd">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.36cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ahiṃsandantamūlāni śarkarām uddhared bhiṣak |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lākṣācūrṇṇair madhuyutais tatastaṃ pratisārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         danta harṣakriyāś cāpi kuryān niravaśeṣataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kapālakaḥ kṛcchratamaḥ tatrāpyeṣā kriyā hitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāyed visrāvaṇaiḥ svinnamacalaṃ krimindakaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāvapīḍair vātaghnaiḥ snehagaṇḍūṣadhāraṇaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhadradārvādivarṣābhūr lepaiḥ snigdhaiś ca bhojanaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         calam uddhṛtya vā sthānaṃ daheta suṣirasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vidārī yaṣṭyāhvaśṛṅgāṭakakaserubhiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.22.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.22.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ daśaguṇakṣīrasiddhaṃ nasya ca pūjitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanurmokṣasamuddiṣṭāṃ kuryāc cārditavat kriyāṃ |</l>

                <div n="23" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 23]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ śophacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra ṣaḍvidhovayavasamutthaḥ śophobhihito lakṣaṇataḥ pratikārataś ca |
                        sarvasaraś ca pañcavidhaḥ | tad yathā | vātapittakaphasaṃnipātaviṣannimittaḥ
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāpatarpitasyābhyarthamadhvagamanādatimātramabhyaharato vā
                        piṣṭānnaharitaśākalavaṇāni | kṣīṇasya vātimātramamlam upasevato
                        mṛtpaktaloṣṭakaṭaśarkarām upaudakamāṃsasevito vā viruddhāhārasya
                        hastyaśvakṣobhanādāyāsitā doṣā dhātūṃ pradūṣayitvā śophamāpādayantyakhile
                        śarīre |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vātapittakaphasannipātaśvayathūnām avayavasamutthe śophalakṣaṇāni
                        vyākhyātāni | viṣanimittas tu garopayogāddu ṣṭatoyasevanāt
                        prakuthitodakāvasekāt saviṣasatvasañcūrṇṇanād vā |
                        saviṣamūtrapurīśaśukraspṛṣṭānāṃ vā tṛṇakāṣṭhādīnāṃ saṃsparśāt || sa tu mṛduḥ
                        kṣiprotthām ca lāvalamvī dāhapākaprāyaś ca bhavati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ śvayathumūrdhvaṃ hi kurvantyāmāśayāśritāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pakvāśayasthā madhye tu varcasthānagatāstvadhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtsnaṃ dehamanuprāptāḥ | kuryuḥ sarvasaran tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yo madhyadeśe śvayathuḥ sa kaṣṭaḥ sarvagaś ca yaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ardhāṅgeriṣṭabhūtaṃ syād yaścordhvaṃ parisarpati |
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaḥ pipāsācchardiś ca daurvalyaṃ jvara eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yasya cānnerucir nāsti śvayathuṃ taṃ vivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi bheṣajaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śophinaḥ sarva eva parihareyuḥ
                        |amlalavaṇamadyaguḍadadhivasātailapiṣṭagurūṇi viśeṣeṇa ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vātaśvayathau trivṛttairaṇḍatailaṃ vā māsam arddhamāsam vā pāyayet |
                        nyagrodhādi siddhaṃ sarpiḥ | pittaśvayathau | āragvadhādisiddhaṃ tailaṃ
                        śleṣmaśvayathau | sannipāśvayathau snuhākṣīrapātratulyaṃ daśabhir
                        amlapātraiḥ | pratisaṃsṛjya dantī dravantī pra tivāyaṃ sarpiḥ pācayitvā
                        pāyayet | viṣanimittamākalpeṣu pratīkāraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ samānyān yogā vakṣyāmaḥ |tilvakaghṛtacaturthāni yānyuktāni
                        udareṣu tatonyatamam upayujyamānaṃ śvayathūnapahanti | mūrttavarttikriyām vā
                        seveta | navāyasaṃ vāharaharmadhunā |
                        viḍaṅgātiviṣākuṭajaphalabhadradārunāgaramaricānāṃ vā dharaṇamuṣṇāmvunā |
                        trikaṭukakṣārayaścūrṇāni triphalākvāthena | mūtram vā tulyakṣīraṃ |
                        harītakīm vā tulyaguḍām upayuñjīta | devadāruśuṇṭhīṃ vā | guggulum vā
                        mūtreṇa | varṣābhūkaṣāyānupānam vā tulyaguḍaṃ śṛṅgaveraṃ | vyoṣaṃ
                        varṣābhūkaṣāyasiddhena vā | sarpiṣāmudgolumvāṃ bhakṣayet |
                        pippalīmūlacitrakacavyāmayūrakavarṣābhūsiddhaṃ vā kṣīraṃ pivet |
                        sahauṣadhamuraṅgīmūlasiddham vā | trikacukair aṇḍaśyāmāmūlasiddham vā |
                        varṣābhūśṛṃgaveradevadārusiddham vā | tathālāvuvibhītakaphalakalkam vā |
                        pippalīmaricaśṛṅgaverānusiddhena ca mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇenālpaṃ snehaṃ bhojayet
                        | yavagodhūmānnaṃ | vṛkṣakārkanaktamālanimvavarṣābhūkvāthaś ca pariṣekaḥ |
                        sarṣapasauvarcalasaindhavaśārṅge ṣṭābhiś ca pradehaḥ kāryaḥ | yathādoṣañ ca
                        tīkṣṇānivamanavirecanāsthāpanānuvāsanāni satatam upaseveta | svedopanāhau ca
                        | sirāś cābhīkṣṇaṃ śoṇitamavasecayet || anyatrapāṇḍuśophāditi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.23.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.23.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭānnamamvlaṃ lavaṇāni madyaṃ mṛdaṃ divāsvapnamajāṅgalañ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         striyo guḍaṃ tailamatho gurūṇi śophaṃ jighāṃsu parivarjayīta ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">ci23|| o ||</p>

                         nāgnivrāhmaṇaprekṣādampatyor antareṇātīyāt | na śavam anuyāyāt |
                        devagovrāhmaṇacaity adhvajarogipatitapāpakarttṛṇāñ ca chāyānnākrāmestaṃ
                        gacchantam udyantam ādityaṃ paśyet | gāṃ dhayantīṃ parasyaṃ vā carantīm
                        parasyai nācakṣīta | nolkāpātātpātendradhanūṣivā | nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamet |
                        nāyo bhūmiṃ vā pāṇipādenābhihanyāt |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.93">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.93</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na vegāndhārayet | na
                        vahirbhāgāṃgrāmanagaradevatāyatanaśmaśānapathasalilāśayasannikṛṣṭhān utsṛjen
                        na prakāśaṃ | na vāyvagnisalilasomārkagogurūṃ pratimukham vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.94">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.94</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhūmiṃ vilikhet | nāsaṃvṛtamukhaḥ sadasi
                        śvāsakāsajṛmbhodbhārakṣavathūnna sṛjet | na
                        paryavaṣṭikāvaṣṭambhapādaprasāraṇāni gurusannidhau kuryāt |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.95">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.95</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na vā karṇṇanasāsrotodaśanavivarāṇyabhiniṣkuṣṇīyāt | na vejayet
                        keśanakhavastragātrāṇi | na gātravaktranakhavāditraḥ kuryāt | na
                        kāṣṭhaloṣṭhatṛṇādīn abhihanyāt | cchindyād bhindyād vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.96">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.96</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nātipravātātapam upaseveta | na muktamātrāgnim upāsīta |
                        notkūṭrakāsanālpāsanān dadhy āsīta | na grīvaṃ viṣamaṃ haret | na
                        viṣamapatitakāyaḥ kriyāṃ seved vased bhuñjīta vā | na pratatamudīkṣeta |
                        viśeṣārjjotirbhāskarasūṣmabalabhrāntāni | na bhāraṃ śirasā vahet | na ca
                        svapnajāgaraṇaśayanāsanasthānacaṅkramanayānavāhanapradhāvanalaghanaprataraṇahāsyabhāṣyavyayāyavyāyāmādīn
                        ucitān apy atimātraṃ seveta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.97">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.97</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ucitād apy ahitāt kramaśo virameta | hitam anucitam apy āseveta kramaśaḥ
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.98">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.98</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nāvākchirāśayīta | na bhinnapātre bhuñjīta | nāñjalipuṭenāpaḥ pivet |
                        kālahitamitasnigdhamadhuraprāyam āhāraṃ vaidyapratyavekṣitam aśnīyāt |
                        grāmagaṇagaṇikāpatitaśatrubhojanāni pariharet | śeṣāṇy api
                        cāniṣṭarūparasagandhaśabdasparśamānasāni anyān evaṃ guṇān api
                        cāsambhramadattāni tāny api na makṣikāvālopahitāni | nāprakṣālitapāṇipādau
                        bhuñjīta | mūtroccārapīḍito vā | na sandhyayor nāpāśrito nātikālahīnam
                        atimātraṃ veti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.99"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.100"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.101"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.102">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.102</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yasmin yasmin ṛtau ye ye doṣāḥ kupyanti dehināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         teṣu teṣu pradātavyā rasās te vijānatā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.103">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.103</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         varṣāsu caturo māsāṃ mātrāvadukaṃ pivet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.104">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.104</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇaṃ himavasante cakāsaṃ grīṣme ca śītalaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hemante ca vasante ca sīdhvariṣṭau piven naraḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.105">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.105</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śritaśītaṃ payo grīṣme prāvṛṭkāle rasaṃ pivet |
                        <caesura/>
                         yūṣaṃ varṣati tasyānte prapivec chītalaṃ jalaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.106">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.106</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svastha eva mato nyas tu doṣāhāgadāturāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehaṃ pippalicūrṇṇena saindhavena ca saṃyutaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.107">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.107</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pived agnivivṛdhyarthaṃ na ca vegāṃ vidhārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         agnidīptir alaṃ nṛṇāṃ rogānāṃ sramanaṃ prati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.108">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.108</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prāvṛṭcharadvasanteṣu samyak snehādim ācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphe pracchardanaṃ pitte viro vastir īraṇe |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.109">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.109</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śasyate triṣvapihito vyāyāmo doṣanāśanaḥ </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.110">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.110</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         utsargamaithunāhāraśodhane syāt tu tanmanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         necchet pratibhayāṃ prāptuṃ pīḍāśārīramānasīṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.111">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.111</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atistrīsaṃprayogāc ca rakṣed ātmānam ātmavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         śoṣakārārśāṃsi śvāsakāśryātipāṇḍutā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.112">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.112</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ativyavāyāj jāyante rogāś cākṣepagādayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyuṣmanto mandajarāvapurvarṇṇavalādhikāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.113">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.113</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sthiropacitamāṃsāś ca bhavanti strīṣu saṃyatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tribhis tribhir ahobhis tu seveta pramamadān naraḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.114">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.114</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣv ṛtuṣu grīṣme tu pakṣāt pakṣād vrajed budhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rajasvalām akāmāñ ca malinām aprajām api |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.115">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.115</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         varṇṇavṛddhām vayovṛddhaṃ tathā vyādhiprapīḍitāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnāṅgīṃ garbhiṇīṃ dveṣyāṃ yonidoṣasamanvitāṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.116">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.116</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sagotrāṃ gurupatnīṃñ ca tathā pravrajitām api |
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhyayoḥ sarvakāle ca nopeyāt pramadān naraḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.117">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.117</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gosarge cārdharātre ca tathā madhyandine pi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         lajjāsamāvahe deśe vivṛte śuddha eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.118">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.118</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣudhito vyādhitaś caiva kṣubdhacittaś ca mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prāptamūtrapurīśaś ca pipāsī durbalas tathā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.119">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.119</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryagyonāv ayonau ca prāptaśukravidhāraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sgaś ca balavān api varjayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.120">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.120</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitān uttānaśayane viśeṣeṇa tu garhitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.121">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.121</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         krīḍayānyaś ca medhāvī hitārthaṃ parivarjayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         rajasvalāṃ prārasyā niyatātmanaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.122">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.122</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭyāyustejasāṃ hāniradharmaś ca tato bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         liṅginīṃ gurupatnīñ ca sagotrām atha parvasu | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.123">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.123</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vṛddhāṃ sandhyayoś cāpi garchato jīvitakṣayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         garbhiṇyāṃ garbhapīḍāsyād vyādhitāñ ca balakṣayaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.124">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.124</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnāṃgīṃ malināṃ dveṣyāṃ kāmāṃ vandhyām asaṃvṛte |
                        <caesura/>
                         deśe śuddhe ca śukrasya manasaś ca kṣayo bhavet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.125">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.125</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣudhitaḥ kṣuvdhacittaś ca madhyāhne tṛṣitobalaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitāyaṃ hānim āpnoti śukraṃ vāyuś ca kupyati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.126">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.126</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhitāyāṃ plīhāmayo mūrcchā doṣaś ca jāyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.127">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.127</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyūṣe cārdharātre ca vātapittaprakupyataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tiryagyonāv ayonau ca duṣṭayonau tathaiva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.128">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.128</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upadaṃśas tathā vāyoḥ kopaḥ syād retasaḥ kṣayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uccārite mūtrite ca retasaś ca vidhāraṇe |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.129">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.129</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uttāne ca bhavec chīghraṃ śukrārśmaryās tu sambhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt sarvaṃ parihared etal lokadvayāhitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.130">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.130</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vayor ūpaguṇo py etāṃ kulya kulānvitāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.131">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.131</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         abhikāmoptikāmāṃś ca hṛṣṭo hṛṣṭām alaṅkṛtāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         seveta pramadān nityaṃ vyājīkaraṇapītavān |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.132">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.132</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkaropahitāṃ bhakṣyāṃ kṣīrañ cāpi saśarkaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyajanaṃ svapnasevā ca vyavāyānte hitāni tu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.24.133">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.24.133</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhamātraṃ samāsena sadvṛttasyetad īritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyur ārogyam artho vā nāsadbhiḥ prāpyate tribhir iti ||</l>

                <div n="25" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 25]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto miśrikacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pālyāmayās tu visrāvyā yaḥ uktāḥ prāṅnibodha tāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paripoṭas tathotpādovamantho duḥkhavardhanaṃḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcamaḥ parilehī ca karṇṇapālyāṃ gadāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saukumāryāc cirotsṛṣṭe sahasābhipravardhite |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇṇaśopho bhavet pālyāṃ sarujaḥ paripoṭavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇāruṇinibhastavdhaḥ savātāt paripoṭakaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gurvābharaṇasaṃyogāt tāḍanod gharṣaṇādibhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophaḥ pālyāṃ bhavec chyāvo dāhapākarujanvitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rakto vā raktapittābhyām unmādaḥ sa gado mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karṇṇaṃ valād vardhayataḥ pālyāṃ vāyuḥ prakupyati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sakaphaṃ prāpya kurute śophaṃ stavdhamavedanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sovamanthaḥ sakaṇḍūko vidāruḥ kaphavātajaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vardhamāne tu durviddha kaṇḍūdāharujānvitaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         śopho bhavati pākaś ca tridoṣo duḥkhavarddhanaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphāsṛkkrimayaḥ kruddhāḥ sarṣapābhāvicāriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kurvanti pālyāṃ srāviṇyaḥ kaṇḍūdāharujānvitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphāsṛkkrimisambhūtaḥ sa visarpānvinatas tanuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lihet saśaṣkuliṃpāliṃ parilehīti sa smṛtaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pālyāmayā hy amī ghorā narasyā
                        <caesura/>
                         mithyāhāravihārasya pāliṃ hiṃsyur upekṣitāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād āśu bhiṣak teṣu snehādikramamācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathābhyaṅgaparīṣekapradehāsṛg vimokṣaṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmānyato viśeṣāc ca vakṣyāmyabhyañjanaṃ prati |
                        <caesura/>
                         kharamaṃḍariyaṣṭyāhvasaindhavāmaradārubhiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         supiṣṭaiḥ sāśvagandhaiś ca mūlakāvalgujāphalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpistailavasāmajjāmadhūcchiṣṭāni cāharet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣīrāṇy atha taiḥpāliṃ pradihyāt paripoṭake |
                        <caesura/>
                         mañjiṣṭhātilayaṣṭyāhvasārivotpalapadmakaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         salodhraiḥ sakadamvaiś ca valājamvvāmrapallavaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhaṃ dhānyāmvlasaṃyuktaṃ tailamutpādanāśanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tālapatryaśvagandhābhyāṃ saindhavāvalgujāphalaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ kulīragodhābhyāṃ vasayā saha sādhitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saralālāṅgalībhyāñ ca hitam unmanthanāśanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         athāśmantakajamvvāmrapatrakvāthaniṣecitāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prapauṇḍīrīkamadhukamañjiṣṭhaṃ rajanīkṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇair durgandhanai pālintailāktām avacūrṇṇayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇair viḍaṅgalākṣābhyāṃ tailaṃ paktvāvacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         svinnāṃ gomayaniḥpiṇḍaiḥ pradihyāt parihike |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇair viḍaṅger athavā praratrīmūtrapeṣimaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karaṇjeṅgudibījair vā kuṭajāragvadhāyutaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvair vā sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ siddhaṃ maricasaṃyutaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sanimvapatrairabhyaṅge madhucchiṣṭānvito hitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhikliṣṭāsu pālīṣu tanvīṣu kaṭhināsu ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         puṣṭyartham mārdavārthañ ca kuryād abhyañjanaṃ śubhaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lopākānūpajāmajjāvasātailaṃ navaṃ ghṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśakṣīraṃ pacet samyagāvāpya madhuraṃgaṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apāmārgāśvagandhā ca tathā lākṣārasaṃ śubhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atha siddhañ ca pūtañ ca svanuguptan nidhāpayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tenābhyañjāt sadā pāliṃ susvinnām atimarditāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etena pālyo vardhante nirujā nirupadravāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdvyaḥ puṣṭāḥ samāḥ snigdhā jāyante bhūṣaṇakṣamāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nīlīpatraṃbhṛṅgarajorjunatvaktṛphalācūrṇṇaṃ sāhacarañ ca puṣpaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmāpuṣpaṃ kṛṣṇapiṇḍītakañ ca sūkṣmañcūrṇṇaṃ sukṛtaṃ yāvad etat |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāvān deyaḥ kardamaḥ paṅkaṣaṇḍāt | paktañcaitat sthāpayellohakumbhyāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         paced etat tilatailena sārdhaṃ datvā kvāthaṃ triphalāmārkavābhyāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         māsādūrdhvaṃ mrakṣaṇenaiva tailaṃ kuryād etat palitaṃ snigdhanīlaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         jamvūpuṣpakārśmarīpārthivañ ca sairīyakaṃ tri</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dvauvarṣābhūśārivākaṇṭakāryau nīlāstilāsrotajañcotpalañ ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         āyaścūrṇṇañcūtapakvasya majjā yaṣṭyāhvāyaṃ mārkavo modayantī |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsīsamagryaṃ sāraś cāsanasya varāhasāhvasya phalañ ca pāṇḍūṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhāgān etāṃ kārṣikāṃ pīṣayitvā sārodakenāsanasyaiva vidvān |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkānetāṃ saptasaptāḍhakeṣu kṣārodakasyākṣatailasya bhāgaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         datvā samyagcellohapātre sthitaṃ pūrvaṃ lohapātre daśāvahaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdupākaṃ sādhitaṃ cāvatārya set pātre bījake vāyase vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraḥ śuddho nasyam etat prayujyāt yathā vatsyāt saṃyato māsamekaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavec ca nityaṃ kṛsaropasevī bhuñjīta cānnaṃ māṣayūṣeṇa cāpi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         māsādūrdhvaṃ tasya keśā bhavanti yāvajjīvaṃ mṛduvat svañjanābhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanty ete nendralupte ca keśāḥ | jarā cainaṃ sahasā nābhyapaiti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balaṃ paraṃ cendriyāṇāṃ labheta sañjāyante nirvalīkañ ca vaktraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etat tailaṃ nāpriyāya pradeyaṃ rājñā deyaṃ kṛṣṇatailaṃ pradhāṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         maniḥśilā haritālaṃ haridre lākṣārodhraṃ gairiko varṇṇakaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         surāṣṭrajākuṣṭhamañjiṣṭhakalkāḥ sapattaṅgārocanā kuṅkumaś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         suvarṇṇāhvāpāṇḍupatraṃ vaṭasya kāleyakaṃ padmakaṃ padmamadhyaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kūcandanaṃ candanaṃ pāratañ ca kākolyādiḥkṣīrapiṣṭaś ca sarvaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vasāmajjā madhūṃcchiṣṭaṃ ghṛtañ ca dugdhaṃ kvāthaḥ kṣīriṇāñ ca drumāṇāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etat sarvam pakvam ekadhyatas tu mukhābhyaṅge sarpir uktaṃ pradhānaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hanyād vyaṅgaṃ nīlikāṃ ca pravṛddhāṃ vaktrejātāḥ piṭakāyāś ca kāścit |
                        <caesura/>
                         padmākāraṃ nirvalīkañ ca vaktraṃ kuryād etat pīnagaṇḍaṃ manojñaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.25.42">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.25.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rājñāmetad yoṣitān cāpi teṣāṃ kuryād vaidyas tat samānāñ ca nityam </l>

                    <p ana="trailer">iti cikitsāsthāna || ❈ ||</p>

                <div n="26" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ kṣīṇavalīyaṃ vyājīkaraṇacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kalasyodagravayaso vyājīkaraṇasevinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣv ṛtuṣv aharahaḥ vyavāyo na nivāritaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         strīṣv akṣaryyaṃ mṛgayatāṃ vṛddhānāñ ca riraṃsatāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         klīvāṇām alpaśukrāṇāṃ strīṣu kṣīṇāś ca ye narāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vilāsinām arthavatāṃ rūpayauvanaśālināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛṇām vahvīpatīnāñ ca yogā vyajīkaro hitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.6"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhojanāni ca citrāṇi pānāni vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vācaḥ srotro nugāminyas tvaksukhasparśanāni ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gandhān manojñaṃ rūpāṇi citrāṇy upavanāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         manasaś cāpratīvāto vyājīkurvanti mānavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tais tair bhāvair ahṛdyais tu riraṃsor manasi kṣate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhvajaḥ pataty adho nṛṇāṃ klaivyaṃ samupajāyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         annair amlvauṣṇalavaṇair atimātropasevitaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saumyadhātukṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ klaivyaṃ tad aparaṃ smṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ativyavāyaśīlo vā na ca vyājīkriyārataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhvajabhaṅgam avāpnoti saśukrakṣayahetukaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         meḍhrarogeṇa mahatā marmcachedena vā punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         klivyaṃ caturtham bhavati nṛṇāṃ puṃstvopaghātajaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.14"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.15</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyānām avaśiṣṭānāṃ kāryo vyājīkaro vidhiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tilamāṣavidārīṇāṃ śālīnāṃ cūrṇṇam eva ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasair ikṣurasair vāpi marditaṃ saindhavānvita |
                        <caesura/>
                         varāhamedasā yuktaṃ ghṛtenotkārikāṃ pacet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāṃ bhakṣayitvā gaccheyuḥ puruṣaḥ ṣaṣṭhim aṅganāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vastrāṇḍasiddhapayasi bhāvitā na sakṛt tilāṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śiśumāravasāpakvā tais tilaiḥ śaṣkulīśubhāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaḥ khādet sa pumāṃ gacchet strīṇāṃ śatam apūrvavat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīlavaṇaupetau vastāṇḍau kṣīrasarpiṣi |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhitau bhakṣayed yas tu sa gacchet pramadāśataṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         māṣapippaliśālīnāṃ yavagodhūmayos tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇabhāgaiḥ samais tais tu ghṛte pūpalikāṃ pacet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāṃ bhakṣayitvā pītvā ca śarkarāmadhuram payaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         naraś caṭakavad gacched daśavārān nirantaraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cūrṇṇaṃ vidāryāḥ sakṛtaṃ svarasenaiva bhāvitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpiḥkṣaudrayutaṃ līḍhvā daśanāryodhirohita ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.24">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.25">

                        <caesura/>
                         etenāśītivarṣo pi yuveva parihṛṣyati ||
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śiśumārasya vā khādet tau tu vyājīkarau bhṛśaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kulīrakūrmanakrāṇām aṇḍāny evaṃ tu bhakṣayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mahiṣarṣabhavastānām pivec chukrāṇi vānaraḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         aśvatthaphalamūlatvaṃ chuṅgasiddham payo 'pi vā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pītvā saśarkkarākṣaudraṃ kuliṅga iva hṛṣyati ||
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.29">

                         udumvararasam pītvā vṛddho 'pi taruṇāyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         māṣāṇām palam ekan tu saṃyuktam madhusarppiṣā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tiṃ līḍhvānupivet kṣīraṃ tena vyājībhavet naraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.26.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nakramūṣikamaṇḍūkacaṭakāṇḍakṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.32">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         yāvan na spṛśate bhūmin tāvad gacchen nirantaraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.33">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.34">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.35"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.26.36"/>

                <div n="27" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 27 (draft based on MS H)</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ sarvvāvādhasaṃśamanīyaṃ rasāyanam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvve vayasi madhye vā manuṣyasya rasāyanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājñaḥ snigdhaśuddhatanoḥ sadā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aviśuddhaśarīrasya yukto rāsāyano vidhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhāti vāsasi kliṣṭe raṅgayoga ivāhitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīrasyopaghātāya doṣajā mānasās tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         upadiṣṭopadeśena teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vāraṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītodakam payaḥ kṣaudraṃ ghṛtamekaikaśo dviśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         triśaḥ samastam athavā prāk pītaṃ sthāpayed vayaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra viḍaṅgataṇḍulam āhṛtya yaṣṭīmadhukamadhuyuktaṃ yathābalaṃ śītatoyena
                        upayuñjīta śītatoyaṃ cānupivet | aharahar mmāsan tad eva madhuyuktaṃ
                        bhallātakakvāthena | drākṣākvāthena vā madhusaṃyuktaṃ |
                        madhvāmalakarasābhyām vā | guḍūcīkvāthena vā | evam ete pañcaprayogā
                        bhavanti | jīrṇṇe mudgayūṣeṇālavaṇena ghṛtaṃntam odanam aśnīyād iti
                        ghṛtavantam odanam aśnīyāt | etaiḥ khalu durnnāmānaḥ kṣayaṃ yāntikrimayaś
                        copaśāmyanti | grahaṇadhāraṇaśaktiś ca bhavati | māsi māsi ca prayoge
                        varṣaśataṃ varṣaśataṃ āyuṣo 'bhivṛddhir vbhavati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍaṅgataṇḍuladroṇaṃ piṣṭapavanapiṣṭavadusvedya vigatakaṣāyaṃ susvinnam
                        avatārya dṛśadi prapiṣṭamāyasyāṃ kumbhyāṃ madhūttarodakaṅ kṛtvā |
                        bhasmarāśau prāvṛṣyabhyatarataś ca catu ro māsānnidadhyāt | varṣāvyavāye
                        coddhṛtyopasaṃskṛtaśarīraḥ sahasrasampātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā prātaḥ
                        prātaryathābalam upayuñjīta | jīrṇṇe mudgayūṣeṇa ghṛtam odanam aśnīyāt |
                        pāṃśuśayyāyāṃ śāyayīta | tasya māsādūrddhaṃ sarvvāṅgebhyaḥ krimayo
                        niḥkrāmanti | tān anutailenābhyaktasya vidalenāpaharet | dvitīye pipīlikās
                        tṛtīye yūkānān tathaivāpaharet | caturthe dantanakharomāṇyavasīryante |
                        pañcame praśasta guṇalakṣaṇāni jāyante | amānuṣañcādityaprakāśam
                        vapuradhigacchati | dūrācchravaṇa darśanāni cāsya bhavati | rajastamasī
                        cāpohya satvamadhitiṣṭhate | śrutanigādī | apūrvvotpādī puṣṭo vṛṣabhavalo
                        'śvajavaḥ punaryuvāṣṭau varṣaśatānyāyuravāpnoti | tasyānutailamabhyaṅgārthe
                        | kaṣāyamājakarṇṇamutsādanārthe | sauśīraṃ kūnūpodakaṃ snānārthe |
                        candanamanulepanārthe | bhallātataka vidhānavadupayogaḥ parihāraś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāśmarīṇānniṣkulīkṛtānāmeṣa eva kalpaḥ | pāṃśuśayyābhojanavarjyaṃ | tatrāpi
                        payasā śritena bhoktavyaṃ | āśiṣaś ca samānāḥ pūrvveṇa |
                        śoṇitapittanimitteṣu vikāreṣveteṣām upayogaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathoktamāgāram praviśya balāmūlārddhapalam palam vā payasyāloḍya pibet |
                        jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ | evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuñjīta tato
                        varṣaśatam vayastiṣṭhati | eṣa eva balātibalānāgabalāvidārīśa tāvarīṇām
                        upayogaḥ | viśeṣatas tu atibalām udakena | nāgabalācūrṇṇaṃ madhukṣīreṇa |
                        śatāvarīmapyevaṃ | pūrvveṇāśiṣaś ca samānāḥ | ete hy auṣadhaprayogāḥ |
                        balakāmānāṃ śoṣiṇāṃ raktapittopasṛṣṭānāṃ śoṇitañccharddayatām viricyamānānāñ
                        copadiśyante ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vārāhīmūlan tulācūrṇṇaṅ kṛtvā tato mātrām madhuyuktam payasāloḍya pibet |
                        jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ | prayogam imam upayevamāno varṣaśatam
                        āyur avāpnoti || strīṣu cākṣayatā | etenaiva cūrṇṇaena
                        payovacūrṇṇāśritaśritaśītam abhimathyājyam utpādya | madhuyuktam upayuñjīta
                        | jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity āhāraḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.27.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cakṣuḥ kāmaḥ prāṇakāmo vā jīvavījakasārāgnimanthamūlāni
                        kvāthairmmāṣaprasthaṃ sādhayet | tasmin sidhyati citrakamūlānāmakṣamātraṃ
                        kalkan dadyāt | āmalakarasacaturvbhāgan tataḥ susvinnam avatārya śītībhūtam
                        madhusarppirbbhyāṃ saṃsṛjyopayuñjīta | jīrṇṇe mudgayūṣeṇā lavaṇena
                        ghṛtavantamodanam aśnīyāt | māsamātramevam anena prayogena ca kṣuḥ
                        sauparṇṇam bhavati | alpabalābalāṃ strīṣu cākṣyyo varṣaśatāyurbbhavati ||
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.27.13"/>

                    <p ana="trailer">cikitsā tha</p>


                </div>

                <div n="28" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 28 (draft based on MS H)</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.1">athāto medhāyuḥkāmīyaṃ rasāyanam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.3">medhāyuḥkāmaḥ śvetāvalgujaphalādy ātapaśuṣkāṇyādāya
                        cūrṇāni kṛtvā guḍena sahāloḍya snehakumbhe nidadhyāt | tataḥ saptarātrād
                        uddhṛtya hṛtadoṣasya yathābalaṃ piṇḍaṃ prayacchet | anuditsūrye, uṣṇodakañ
                        cānupibet | bhallātakavidhānavac cāgārapraveśaḥ | jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe
                        vihimābhir adbhiḥ | pariṣiktagātraḥ śālīnāṃ ṣaṣṭikānām vā payasā
                        śarkarāmadhureṇaudanam aśnīyāt | evaṃ ṣaṇmāsān upayuñjya vigatapāpmā
                        valopetaḥ śrutanigādī bhavati | kuṣṭharogiṇām udariṇām vā kṛṣṇāni
                        gomūtrāloḍyārddhapalikaṃ piṇḍam udite sūrye pāyayet | sāyāhne
                        cālavaṇenāmalakayūṣeṇa sarpiṣmantam odanam aśnīyāt | evaṃ māsam upayujya
                        smṛtimān arogo varṣaśatāyur bhavati | eṣa evopayogaś citrakamūlānāṃ rajanyāś
                        ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.4"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāram praviśya maṇḍūkaparṇīsvarasam ādāya
                        sahasrasampātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalam payasāloḍya pibet | tilair vā saha
                        bhakṣayet | payo 'nupānaṃ | jīrṇe payaḥ sarpirodana ity āhāraḥ | bilvamātram
                        vā pi piṇḍam payasāloḍya pibet | evan daśarātram upayujya medhāvī
                        varṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.5"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāram praviśya pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhakto
                        brāhmīsvarasamādāya sahasrasampātābhihutaṃ kṛtvā yathābalam prayuñjītau |
                        jīrṇauṣadhaś cāparāhṇe yavāgūmalavaṇam pibet || kṣīrasātmyo 'thavā payasā
                        bhuñjīta || evaṃ saptarātram upayujya vrahmavarccasī medhāvī bhavati |
                        dvitīyaṃ saptarātram upayujya grantham īpsitam utpādayati naṣṭañ cāsya
                        prādur bhavati | tṛtīyam uccāritaṃ śatam apy avadhārayati | evam
                        ekaviṃśatirātram upayujya lakṣmīr apakrāmati | śarīrāt mūrttimatī cainam
                        vāgdevīm anupraviśati | sarvāś cainaṃ śrutayo 'vatiṣṭhate | śrutidharaḥ
                        pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati || </l>

                    <p xml:id="SS.4.28.6"> vrahmīsvarasaprasthadvaye ghṛtaprastham viḍaṅgataṇḍulānāṅ
                        kuḍavam vacābhṛ vṛtayoḥ | dvādaśa dvādaśa ca harītakyāmalakavibhītakāni
                        kalkapiṣṭānyavāpyaikadhyaṃ sādhayitvā svanuguptan nidadhyāt | tataḥ
                        pūrvvavad yathābalam upayuñjīta | jīrṇṇapūrvvavad āhāraḥ parihāraś ca |
                        etenordhvam adhaś ca krimayogacchanti | alakṣmīra apakrāmati |
                        puṣkaravarṇṇaḥ śrutanigādī trivarṣaśatāyur bhavati | etad eva
                        viṣakuṣṭhaviṣamajvaram apasmāronmādabhūtagraheṣu saṃśodhanam upadiśanti | </p>



                    <p xml:id="SS.4.28.7"> hṛtadoṣa evāgāram praviśya haimavatyā vacāyāḥ piṇḍam
                        āmalakamātram abhihutan kṛtvā payasālo pivet | jīrṇṇe payaḥ sarppirodana ity
                        āhāraḥ | evaṃ dvādaśarātram upayuṃjīta | tato 'sya śrotraṃ vidhiyate |
                        dvirabhyāsāt smṛtimān bhavati | trirabhyasya śrutam ādhatte |
                        caturdvādaśarātram abhyasya tatas tārkṣyan darśanam utpadyate | śatāyuś ca
                        bhavati | dve pale itasyā vacāyāḥ kvāthyam pivet payasā pūrvvaśāśiṣaś ca
                        samānāḥ | </p>


                    <p xml:id="SS.4.28.8"> vacāśatapākam vā sarppir droṇam upayñjya
                        pañcavarṣaśatāyur bhavati | galagaṇḍāpacīślīpadasvararabhedāṃś cāpahanti ||
                        bhavanti || </p>



                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.9"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.10"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.11"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.12"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.24"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.25"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.26"> pāpmānam upahanty etāḥ śriyaṃ dadyut tathāuṣadhīḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryun nāgabalam vāpi manuṣyam amaropamaṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.27"> satatādhyayanam vādaḥ paratantrāvalokanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tad vidyācāryasevā ca buddhimedhākarāḥ gaṇaḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.28.28"> āyuṣyaṃ bhojanañ jīrṇṇe vegānāñ ca vidhāraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
