                <div n="29" type="adhyāya">

                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 29 (draft based on MS H)</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ svabhāvavyādhipratiṣedhanīyaṃ rasāyanam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vrahmā yadajṛt pūrvvamamṛtaṃ somasaṃjñitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jarāmṛtyuvināśāya vidhānan tasya vakṣyate||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         eka eva khalu bhagavān somaḥ sthānānām ākṛtir vviśeṣaiś caturvviṃṅśatidhā
                        bhidyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tadyathā || aṃśumān mūñjavām̐ś caiva candramārajataprabhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratānavām̐s tālavṛntaḥ karavīrāṅśusannibhāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         svayamprabho mahāsomo yaś cāpi garuḍāhṛtaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gāyatryas traiṣṭubhaḥ pāṃktyo jāgrataḥ sātkaras tathā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         agniṣṭomo revataś ca yaś coktha iti saṃjñitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gāyatryā tripadā yukto yaś coḍupatir ucyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ete somāḥ samākhyātā vedoktair nnāmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvveṣām eva caiteṣāmeko vidhir upāsane ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvve tulyaguṇāś caiva vidhānaṃ sampravakṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atho nyatama somam upayuyuṃkṣuḥ sarvvopakaraṇaparicārakopetaḥ | praśaste
                        deśe trivṛtamagāraṅkārayitvā hṛtadoṣaḥ pratisaṃsṛṣṭabhaktaḥ praśaste
                        tithikaraṇamuhūrttaṅaaśumantam ādāyādhvarakalpenābhiṣṭutya
                        yathoktāgāraskṛtamaṅgalaḥ | somacandraṃkandaṃsuvarṇṇasūcyā vidārya payo
                        gṛhṇīyāt | sauvarṇṇe rājate pātreñjalimātraṃ tato sakṛdevopa yuñjīto
                        nāsvādayamānas ta upaspṛśya śeṣam apsv astv avasādya yam aniyamābhyāmātmānaṃ
                        saṃyojya vāgyato 'bhyantaraḥ | suhṛdbhir anvāsyamāno viharet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanam pītavāṃs tu nirvvāte niyatātmanā
                        <caesura/>
                         śucirāsītastiṣṭheccaṃkrampānna kathañcana samviśet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na cātmānam ādarśe syu vā nirīkṣeta | rūpaśālitvāt tato nyaddaśarātraṃ
                        krodhādīn parihared eṣa sarveṣām upayogaḥ | viśeṣatas tu
                        vallīpratānakṣupādayaḥ somā bhakṣayitavyāḥ | bhavanti teṣāṃmavacaturtho
                        muṣṭayaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṅśumantaṃ sauvarṇṇo pātrebhiṣuśayāc candramasaṃ rājate |
                        tāvupayojyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam avāpyaiśānaṃ devaṃ paśyati | śeṣāṃs tu
                        tāmramaye mṛnmaye vā śūdravarjyañ ca tribhir varṇṇaiḥ soma upayoktavyaḥ |
                        tataś caturthe māsi paurṇṇamāsyāṃ vrāhmaṇamarcayitvā kṛtamaṅgalā niḥkramya
                        yatheṣṭaṃ vrajediti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         oṣadhīnāṃ patiṃ somam upayujyaivam akṣata |
                        <caesura/>
                         daśavarṣasahasrāṇi navān dhārayate tanuṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nāgnir na tejaṃ na viṣaṃ na śastraṃ nāśastram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyālamāyuḥ kṣapaṇe samarthāni bhavanti hi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhadrāṇāṃ ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇāṃ prasūtānāmanekadhā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuñjarāṇāṃ sahasrasya balaṃ samadhigacchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrodaṃ śakrasadanaṃ uttarāṃś ca kurūn api
                        <caesura/>
                         yatrecchati sa gantuṃ vai tatrāsyāpratighāsatiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṃdarpa iva rūpeṇa kantyā candra ivāparaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prahlādayati bhūtānāṃ manāṃsi sa mahādyutiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sāṃgopāṃgāṃś ca nikhilāṃ vedāṃ viṃdati tatvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraty amoghasaṅkalpo devavaccākhilaṃ jagat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarveṣām eva somānāṃ patrāṇi daśa pañca ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tāni śukle ca kṛṣṇe ca jāyante ca patanti ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ekaikaṃ jāyate patraṃ somasyāharahas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklasya pūrṇṇamāsyān tu bhavet pañcadaśacchadaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         divase divase patramekaikaṃ śīryate punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇadvayaṃ cāpi latā bhavati kevalā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṃśumānājyagandhas tu kandavān rajataprabhaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kadalyākārakandas tu muñjavān laśunacchadaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         candramā rajatābhāso jale carati sarvadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         garuḍāhṛtanāmā ca śyenākhyau cāpi pāṇḍurau |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarpanirmokasadṛśau tau vṛkṣā grāvalamvinau |
                        <caesura/>
                         athānye maṇḍalaiś citraiś citritā iva bhānti te |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīrakandalatāvantaḥ patrairnānāvidhairvṛtā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         himavaty arvude sahye mahendre malaye tathā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāriyātre ca vindhye ca devasūte hṛde tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttareṇa vitastāyāḥ prabhavasya mahīdharāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.28.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.28.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañca teṣām ato madhye sindhur nāma mahāhradaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         haṭhavat plavate tatra candramā somasattamaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyoddeśeṣu cāpy asti muñjavān aṃśumān api |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaśmīre ca saro yantu nāmnā kṣudrakamānasaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gāyatryaśtraiṣṭubhaś cāpi jāgrataḥ satkaras tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra santyapare cāpi somāḥ somasamaprabhāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.29.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.29.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na tāṃ paśyanty adharmiṣṭhāḥ kṛtaghnāś cāpi ye narāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bheṣajadveṣiṇaś cāpi vrāhmaṇadveṣiṇas tatheti ||</l>

                <div n="30" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 30]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.30.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto nivṛttasantāpīyaṃ rasāyanaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.30.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā nivṛttasantāpā modantedivi devatāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathauṣadhyastvimāḥ prāpya modante bhuvi mānavāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.30.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha khalu saptavidhāḥ puruṣā rasāyanaṃ nopayuñjīran | tad yathā |
                        anātmavānalaso daridraḥ pramādī vyasanī pāpiṣṭho bheṣajāpamānī ceti ||
                        saptabhiḥ kāraṇair na saṃpadyante | tad yathā |
                        ajñānādarambhādasthiracittatvād dāridrādanāyatanādāyāsādauṣadhālābhācceti
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.30.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athauṣadhīn vakṣyāmaḥ | tatrājagarī svetakāpotī gonasī kṛṣṇakāpotī vārāhī
                        cchatrāticchatrā kanyā kareṇu ajā takrakād ity aparṇṇinī vrahmasuvarcalā
                        mahāsrāvaṇī golāmī mahāvegavatī cetyaṣṭādaśa somasamavīryāmahauṣadhayo
                        vyākhyāḥ || tatra tāsāṃ somavat kriyāsīstutatayaḥ śāstrebhihitāḥ |
                        tāsāmagārebhihitānāṃ yāḥ kṣīravatyastāsāṃ kṣīrakuḍavaṃ sakṛdevopuyañjīta |
                        yāstvakṣīrāmūlavatyastāsāṃ pradeśinī pramāṇānī trīṇi kāṇḍāni pramāṇam
                        upayoge | svetakāpotī samūlavṛttā bhakṣayitavyā | gonasyājagarī
                        kṛṣṇakāpotīnāṃ sanakhaṃ muṣṭiṃ kāṇḍasaḥ kalpayitvā kṣīreṇa visrāvya
                        pratisāritamabhighāritamabhihutañ ca sakṛdevopayuñjīta | tatastāsāṃ
                        yānyāpayasā sakṛdeva vrahmasuvarcalā saptarātram upayoktavyā | bhakṣakalpena
                        | śeṣāṇāṃ pañca pañca palāni kṣīrāḍhakakathitāni prasthevaśiṣṭe parisrāvya
                        sakṛdevopayuñjīta | somena cāhāravihārāḥ vyākhyātāḥ | kevalaṃ tu
                        navanītamabhyaṃ gārthe | śeṣaṃ somavadānirgamāditi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.30.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.30.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bha || yuvānaṃ sihaṃvikrāntaṃ sakṛcchrubhanigāditaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryuretāḥ krameṇaivaṃ dvisahasrāyuṣaṃ naraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ snehopayogacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.3"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dviyoniścaturvikalpobhihitaḥ snehaḥ snehaguṇāś ca | tatra jaṅgamebhyo
                        gavyaṃ snehaṃ pradhāṇatamaṃ sthāvarebhyas tilasneha iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ yathāprayojanato yathāpradhānataś ca | sthāvarasnehāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
                        | tatra
                        tilvakairaṇḍakuśāmradantīpalāśaśaṅkhinīviṣāṇigavākṣīkampilyakaśampākanīlinīsnehā
                        virecayanti |. jīmūtakakūṭajakṛtavedhanekṣvākumadanasnehā vāmayanti |.
                        viḍaṅgasthū lamañjarīmadhuśigrusūryavallīpīlusiddhārthakajyotiṣmatīsnehāḥ
                        śiro virecayanti | karañjapūtīkalavaṇamātuluṅgeṅgudīkirātatiktakasnehāḥ
                        duṣṭavraṇeṣūpayojyāḥ |. turuvakakapitthabhallātakapaṭolasnehāḥ mahāvyādhiṣu
                        |. trapusatvārukerkāratumvurukaṣmāṇḍasnehāḥ mūtrasaṅgeṣu
                        ||kapotavaṅkaharītakīsnehāḥ śarkarārśmariṣu |.
                        kusumbhasarṣapātasīpicumardātimuktakakāṇḍīrasnehāḥ prameheṣu |.
                        nāḍīkerapanasapiyālavilvamadhūka śleeṣmātakasnehāḥ pittasaṃsṛṣṭe vāyau ||
                        vibhītakapiṇḍītakabhallātakasnehāḥ kṛṣṇīkaraṇeṣu |. śravaṇakaṃgukasnehāḥ
                        pāṇḍūkaraneṣu | saralāpītadāruśiṃśapāsanasārasnehāḥ dardrukiṭibheṣu | sarva
                        eva snehā vātam upahanti | tailaguṇāḥ samāsena vyākhyātāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ kaṣāyapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra kecidāhus tvak
                        patrapuṣpaphalādīnāṃ bhāgastaccaturguṇamudakaṃ caturthāṃśāvaśeṣitaṃ
                        kvāthyāvatārayed ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ | tat tu na samyak kasmād
                        āgamasiddhatvāt </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         palakuḍavādīnām ity etac copadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra dvādaśadhānyamāṣā madhyamā
                        suvarṇṇamāṣakaste śoḍaṣasuvarṇṇāḥ | ataścordhvaṃ caturguṇamabhivardhayataḥ
                        palakuḍavaprasthāḍhakadroṇā abhiniṣpadyante | tulā punaḥ palaśataṃ tābhir
                        viṃśatir bhāraḥ śuṣkāṇām ārdrāṇāṃ dravāṇāṃ ca dviguṇam iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehakukuḍavesāṇyakvāthyadravyadurvyaprastho vidheyas taccaturguṇamudakaṃ
                        caturthāṅgāvaśeṣitaṃ kvāthyāvatārayed ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ |
                        snehakuḍavesāṇya bheṣajapalaṃ kalkam iṣṭaṃ caturguṇañ ca kaṣāyam āvāpya
                        vipaced ity eṣa snehapākakalpa iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.9</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāyaṃ vidhir āstheyo nirdiṣṭe tadvad eva tu ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.10</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ snehapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ | sa tu pākas tṛvidho
                        mṛduścikkanaḥ kharacikkaṇa iti | dhavivekamātraṃ yatra bheṣajaṃ sa mṛduḥ |
                        madhūcchiṣṭamivalepayati yatra bheṣajaṃ sa cikkaṇaḥ | phenāni mātra vailasya
                        śeṣaṃ ghṛtavadādiśet kṛṣṇamavasannamīṣadviśadaṃ cikkaṇaṃ ca yatra sa
                        kharacikkaṇa iti |. ata ūrdhvaṃ pradagdhasneha bhavati | taṃ punaḥ sādhayet
                        | tatra pānābhya va nasyābhyañjanīyaś cikkaṇaḥ | vastisnehāḥ kharacikkaṇa
                        iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.12">

                        yathābalaṃ tailasya ghṛtasya vā mātraṃ prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.25ab"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.25cd">

                        <caesura/>
                         yā mātrā parijīryeta caturbhāgagate na hi</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sā mātrā dīpayatyagnim alpadoṣe ca pūjitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yā mātrā parijīryeta tatrārdhadivase gate </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.31.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sā vṛṣyāvṛṃhaṇīyā ca madhyadoṣe ca pūjitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yā mātrā parijīryeta caturbhāgāvaśeṣite</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.28">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.29">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.30">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.31">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.32">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.33ab">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.40"/>

                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 32]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra caturvidhaḥ svedā bhavati |. tad yathā tāpasvedo bāṣpasvedaḥ
                        |upanāhasvedo dravasvedaś ceti | tatra svedavikalpāvarodhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tāpasvedo nāmapālikāṃ sakandaphalavāṃlikāvastraiḥ prayujyate
                        śayānasya bāṣpatāpoṅgāraiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bāṣpasvedas tu kapālapāṣāṇoṣṭakalohapiṇḍān agnivarṇān adbhir
                        āsicyatairārdravastrapariveṣṭitaiḥ | svedayed aṅgapradeśā evaṃ
                        māṃsarasapayodadhisnehadhānyāmvlavātaharapatrabhaṃgakvāthapūrṇṇam vā kumbhīm
                        abhiprataptāṃ prāvṛtyoṣmāṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | pārśvacchidreṇa vā kumbhena tasyāḥ
                        kumbhyāmukhena mukhamabhis andhāya tasminañchidrehastiśuṇḍākāraṃ nāḍīṃ
                        praṇidhāya śayānaṃ svedayet</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhopaviṣṭaṃ svabhyaktaṃ prāvṛtam vā |. bha ||
                        <caesura/>
                         hastiśuṇḍikayā nāḍyā svedayed vātarogiṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaṃ sarvānugā hyeṣā na ca saṃkleṣayen naraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāmārdhamātratrivakrahastihastasamākṛtiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedanārthe hitā nāḍī kailiñjī hastiśuṇḍikā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.8ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣāyāmamātram vā bhūmim utkīrya khādiraiḥ </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8cd">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.8cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāṣṭair avadāhyābhyukṣya vātahara</l>

                    <l met="hypermetrical" xml:id="SS.4.32.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.9" met="hypermetrical</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         patrabhaṅgairavacchādya śayānaṃ svedayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śilātalamavadāhyāpohya bhasmaṃ ca pūrvavat |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kuṭīm vā caturdvārāṃ kṛtvā tasyām upaviṣṭasyāntaś caturvāṃgārān
                        anuparidhāya svedayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāśadhānyāni vā samyagusvedyāstīrya kiliñjenyasmiṃ vā tatpratirūpake
                        śayānaṃ svedayed evaṃ pāṃśu gośakṛttuṣapa lāloṣmabhiḥ svedayed iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upanāhasvedas tu vātaharadravyakalkair amvlapiṣṭair lavaṇapragāḍhaiḥ
                        susnigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiś ca pradihya svedayed evaṃ kākolyādirelāsu rasādim
                        āhṛtya tilātasīsarṣapakalkair vā kṛsaraveśavārapāyasotkārikābhir vā etābhir
                        eva vāyo dūlikāṃ vadhvā svedayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravasvedas tu vātaharadravyakvāthapūrṇṇakoṣṭakaṭāhe droṇyām vāvagāhya
                        svedayet | evaṃ payomāṃsarasayūṣatailaghṛtadhānyāmvlamūtreṣvetair eva
                        sukhoṣṇaiḥ pariṣiñcediti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tāpoṣmāsvede viśeṣataḥ śleṣmaghnau | upanāhasvedo vātaghnaḥ |
                        anyatarasmiṃ pittasaṃsṛṣṭadravasveda iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.15"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvidho yo 'bhihito dvādhā svedaḥ prayujyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         svasminn eva dehe tu dehasyāvayave tathā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yeṣān nasyaṃ vidhātavyaṃ bastiś cāpi hi dehināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanīyāś ca ye kecit pūrvaṃ svedyās tu me matāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         paś cāt svedyāhṛte śalye mūḍhagarbhānupadravā |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyak prajātā kāle ca paś cāt svedyaiva jānatāṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvāṃ svedyā paś cāc ca bhagandaryarśaśas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmaryāṃ cāturo jantu śeṣāñcāstre pravakṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nānabhyakte nāpi cā snigdhadehe yojyaḥ svedyaḥ svedavidbhiḥ kathañcit |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭaṃ loke kāṣṭham asnigdhamāśur yāyāt bhaṅgaṃ svedayogair gṛhītaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedaklinnā dhātusaṃsthā tu doṣāḥ svasthānasthā ye ca mārgeṣu līnāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyak svedair yojitais te dravatvaṃ prāptāḥ koṣṭhaṃ śodhanair yātyaśeṣāḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         agne dīptin mārdavaṃ tvakprasādaṃ bhaktaśraddhāṃ srotasāṃ nirmalatvaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāt svedas tandrīnidre ca hanyāt | sandhīm katvāṃśceṣṭayed āśuyuktaḥ
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedāsrāvo vyādhihānirlaghutvaṃ śītārthitvaṃ mārdavaṃ cāturasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaksvinne lakṣaṇaṃ prāhuretat | mithyāsvinne viparītaṃ tad eva ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sphoṭotpattiḥ pittaraktaprakopo madāmūrcchābhramadāho klamaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         atisvinne sandhipīḍā ca tṛṭca śītā kriyās tatra kuryād vidhijñaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍumehī raktapittī tṛṣārttaḥ kṣutakṣīṇo durvalo jīrṇṇabhaktaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dakodarīgarbhiṇī pānapañca naite svedyā yaścamartyotisārī |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedād eṣā yāṃti dehāvināśaṃ asādhyatvaṃ yānti caiṣāṃ vikārāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedaiḥ sādhyo durvalojīrṇṇabhaktā yadi syātāṃ svedanīyau tatastau |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.26"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvasvedāṃ nivāte tu jīrṇṇānne cāvacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehābhyaktaśarīrasya śītair ācchādya cakṣuṣī |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atisvinnam athāsvābhya śītāṃbutrāsanaṃ hitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snānam uṣṇāmbunā caiva nivatañcālayayet |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29ab"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29cd">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.32.29cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhojayec cānabhiṣyandi sarvaṃ vācāram ādiśed iti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">ci|| ❈||</p>

                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 33]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vamanavirecanasādhyopakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ calitāḥ praśamayitavyāḥ pravṛddhā nirhattavyāḥ
                        svasthānasthārakṣyā iti siddhāntaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prādhānyena vamanavirecanenirharaṇe varttate | tasmāt tayor vidhānam
                        ucyamānam upadhārayasva |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathāturaṃ snigdhasvinnam anabhiṣyandibhir āhārair anavabaddhadoṣam
                        ālocya svo vamanaṃ pāyayitāsmīti saṃbhojayet | saṃbhojyas tu tīkṣṇāgnir
                        balavān bahudoṣo mahāvyādhiparigṛhīto vamanasātmyaś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         peśalair vividhairannair doṣamutkliśya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnāya vamanaṃ dattaṃ samyak pravarttate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāparedyuḥ pūrvāhṇe sādhāraṇe kāle
                        vamanadravyakaṣāyakalkacūrṇṇasnehanānyatamasya mātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        asātmyabībhatsadudarśanadurgandhāni vāmanīyāni vidadhyād ato viparītāni |.
                        tatra sukumārāṃ kṛśaṃ bālaṃ vṛddhāṃ bhīrum vā vamanasādhyavikāreṣu
                        kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭhaṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        pītauṣadhañcapāṇibhir agnitaptair upaspṛśyamānaṃ muhūrttam upekṣeta | tatra
                        pravṛttahṛllāsaṃ jñātvā jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭam anyena hṛtpṛṣṭhayoḥ pāṇibhyāṃ
                        uparigṛhītam aṅguligandharvahastapatravṛttotpalanālānām anyatamena
                        kaṇṭhamanabhis pṛśan vāmayet yāvat samyag vāntalakṣaṇāni bhavanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaprasekaṃ hṛdayāviśuddhiṃ kaṇḍūñ ca duścharditaliṅgam āhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittātiyogañ ca visaṅjñatāñ ca hṛtkaṇṭhapīḍām api cātivānte |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte kaphasyāndramukhaṃ pravṛtte śuddheṣu hṛtkaṇṭhaśirassu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghau ca dehe kaphasaṃsrave ca sthite suvāntaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavavasyet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samyagvāntaṃ cainam abhis amīkṣya snaihikavairecanikopaśamanīyānāṃ dhūmānām
                        anyataṃ sāmarthyataḥ pāyayitvā cārikam upadiśet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato parāhṇe suvibhaktadeham uṣṇābhir ahniḥ pariṣiktagātraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulattham udgaḍhakijāṅgalānāṃ yuṣai rasair vāpy upabhojayīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaprasekaḥ svarabhedatandrā nidrāsyadaurgandhyaviṣopasargāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurutvakaṇḍūgrahaṇīpradoṣā na santijantorvamataḥ kadācit |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         chinne tarau puṣpaphalaprarohā yathāvināśaṃ sahasā vrajanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāhṛte śleṣmaṇi ccharddanena tajjā vikārā vilayaṃ vrajanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na vāmayet taimirikannagulminaṃ na caivapāṇḍūdararogapīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlakṣatakṣīṇakṛśātivṛddhā narśorditā kṣepakapīḍitāṃś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣaṃ pramehe taraṇe ca garbhe gacchatyadhordhvaṃ rudhire ca tīvre |
                        <caesura/>
                         tuṣṭe ca koṣṭhe krimibhir manuṣyaṃ na vāmayed varcasi cātivṛddhe ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.16"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ete py ajīrṇṇavyathitā vāmyā ye ca viṣāturāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atīvacolbaṇakaphās te ca syur madhukāmbunā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.18"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanam api snigdhasvinnāya ca deyaṃ | avāntasya hi samyagviriktasyāpi
                        satovasrastaḥ śleṣmāgra haṇīñ chādayati | gauravam āpādayati pravāhikām vā
                        kurute | tasmāt snigdhasvinnāya vāntāya ca deyam |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāturaṃ svo virecanaṃ pāyayitāsmīti pūrvāhṇe laghubhojayet |
                        phalāmvlamuṣṇodakaścainamanupāyayet | athāparehani vigataśleṣmadhātāvāt
                        uropakramaṇīyād apekṣyāturam athāsmai virecanaṃ mātrāṃ prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra mṛduḥ krūro madhya iti trividhaḥ koṣṭho bhavati | tatra bahupitto
                        mṛduḥ sa dugdhenā viricyate | bahuvātaśleṣmā krūro durvirecyaḥ | sagadoṣo
                        madhyaḥ sādhāraṇa iti | tatra mṛdau mṛdvī mātrā | tīkṣṇakrūre | madhye
                        madhyā karttavyeti | pītauṣadhaś ca tanmanāḥ śayyābhyāse viricyeta | na
                        prāptavegaṃ vidhārayet | na cāprāptaṃ prāṇenākāṃkṣeta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.22"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ca vamane krameṇa prasekauṣadhaḥ pittānilāgacchanty evaṃ virecane
                        vātamūtrapurīṣapittakaphā iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bha ||hṛtkukṣyaśuddhiḥ paridāhakaṇḍūviṇmūtrasaṃgaś ca na sadvirikte |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāgudabhraṃśakaphātiyogāḥ śūlodgamāś cātiviriktaliṅgaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gateṣu doṣeṣu kaphāntakeṣu glānyelaghutve manasaś ca tuṣṭau |
                        <caesura/>
                         gatenile cāpy anulomabhāvaṃ samyagviriktaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavasyet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mandāgnimakṣīṇamasadviriktaṃ na pāyayet tad divasaṃ yavāgūṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaṃ tṛṣārttaṃ suvirecitaś ca tanvī sukhoṣṇaṃ laghu pāyayīta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         buddheḥ prasādaṃ balamindriyāṇāṃ dhātusthiratvaṃ jvalanābhivṛddhiṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti virecanaṃ samyagupāsyamānaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathodakānāṃ tu vijaṅgamānāṃ rodhevadīrṇṇe dhruva eva nāśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte hṛtendhevam upadravāṇāṃ pittātmikākānāṃ vihito vināśaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇāḥkṛśārūkṣitabālavṛddhādīnotha śoṣī bhayaśokataptaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śāntas tṛṣārtto parijīrṇṇabhakto garbhiṇyadho gacchati yasya cāsṛk |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         navapratiśyāyaparītadeho navajvarīyā ca navaprasūtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyan ity āna virecanīyā snehādibhir ye tv anupaskṛtāś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atyarthapittābhiparītadehāṃ virecayet tān api mandamandaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanair yāṃti narā vināśam ajñaprayuktair avirecanīyā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.32"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saratvasaukṣmyataikṣṇyoṣṇe vikāśitvād virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanaṃ tu hareddoṣāṃ samyaguktaṃ vṛthānyathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mādāya pyamānaṃ virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇodrekād vrajedūrdhvam apakvaṃ vamanaṃ punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.35">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdukoṣṭhasya dīptāgner dattaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na samyag nirhared doṣān ativegapradhāvitaṃ |</l>

                    <l met="hypermetrical" xml:id="SS.4.33.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.36" met="hypermetrical</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prātar yad auṣadhaṃ pītaṃ bhaktapākasame kṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         paktaṃ gacchati doṣāṃs tu nirharen niravaśeṣataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         durbalasya naḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         haret prabhūtānalpāṃs tu samayet pracyutānatha |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hareddoṣāṃ calān pakvaṃ balino durbalasya vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         calā hy upekṣitā doṣāḥ kleśayeyuś ciran naraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mandāgniṃ krūrakoṣṭhañ ca sakṣāralavaṇairghṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sandhukṣitāgni snigdhañ ca svinnañcaiva viśodhayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnasya bhaiṣajyair doṣas tu kleśito bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cālīyeta mārgeṣu snigdhe bhāṇḍa ivodakaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na cātisnigdhakāyāya dadyāt snerhavirecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ pracyāvitā bhūyo līyante tena vartmasu |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.42"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.43">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         virūkṣya snehasātmyantu bhūyaḥ saṃsnehya recayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tena doṣā hṛtās tasya bhavanti snehabandhanāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.44">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prāgadhītauṣadhaṃ śodhya pāyayet mṛduśodhaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tato vijñātakoṣṭhasya kāryaṃ saṃśodhaṇaṃ punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.45">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaṃ dṛḍhaphalaṃ hṛdyam alpamātraṃ mahāguṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāpat svalpātyayañ cāpi piben nṛpatir auṣadhaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.46">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehasvedāvakṛtvāgre yas tu saṃśodhanaṃ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         dāru śuṣkamivānāme dehas tasya viśīryate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.47">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.33.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehasvedapracalito rasaiḥ snigdhair udīritā |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ koṣṭhagatā jantoḥ sukhaṃ hartuṃ virecanair iti ||</l>

                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 34 (draft based on MS H)</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vamanavirekavyāpaccikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyāturanimittam vamanam virecanañ ca || pañcadaśadhā vyāpadyate tatra
                        vamanasyādho gacchaty ūrddhvam virecanasya | sāmānyam ubhayoḥ
                        sāvaśeṣauṣadhatvam alpadoṣahṛtatvaṃ jīrṇṇauṣadham vātaśūlam ayogātiyogau
                        jīvādānamādhmānam parikarttaḥ parisrāvaḥ pravāhikā hṛdayasaraṇa vibandha iti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra bubhukṣāpīḍitasya tīkṣṇāgner mmṛdukoṣṭhasya vāvatiṣṭhamānaṃ
                        durvvāntasya vā guṇasāmānyād vamanam adho gacchati | tatrepsitān avāptir
                        ddoṣo kleśaś ca tam āśusnehayitvā bhūyastīkṣṇatarair vvāmayet iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apariśuddhāmāśayasyotkliṣṭaśleṣmaṇaḥ sāvaśeṣān nasya vā'hṛdyam
                        bahudhāvacāritam vā virecanam ūrddham tiṣṭhati tatrepsitān avāptibastidoṣān
                        kleśatamulbaṇaśleṣmāṇamāśu || 1|| vāmayitvā bhūyas tīkṣṇatarair vvirecayet
                        iti | āmāśaye tvāmavat samvidhānaṃ | ahṛdyetiprabhūte ca hṛdyam
                        pramāṇayuktañ ca | tathā tathāpy uttiṣṭhati tṛtīye nna pāyayet ataś cainam
                        madhughṛtaphāṇitayuktairllehayitvā virecayet iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣavigrathitamalpamauṣadham avasthitamūrddhabhāgikam adhobhāgikam vā na
                        sraṃsayatidoṣān | tatra
                        tṛṣṇāpārśvaśūlañccharddimūrcchāparvvabhedohṛllāsorucirudgarāviśuddhiś ca
                        bhavati | tam uṣṇābhir adbhir āśu vāmayet | ūrddhvabhāgikam adhobhāgikam vā
                        sāvaśeṣauṣadham apradhāvitadoṣam atibalamasamyag viriktalakṣaṇam upayuktam
                        alpam apy evam vāmayet iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         krūrakoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇāgner alpamapyauṣadham alpaguṇam vā bhaktavat pākam
                        upaiti | tatra samudīrṇṇa doṣāḥ | yathākālam anirhriyamāṇā vibhramaṃ
                        kurvvanti | tamanalpamamandañcauṣadham pāyayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnenālpam alpaguṇam vā bheṣajam upayuktam alpān doṣān harati |
                        taddoṣaśeṣam vamanagauravam upakleśa hṛdayāṃ viśuddhiṃ vyādhivivṛddhiñ ca
                        karoti roga)| tatra yathāyogam pāyayitvā vāmayed dṛḍhataraṃ |
                        virecanadoṣaśeṣaṃ gudaparikarttam ādhmānaṃ gauravamanisaraṇam vāyor
                        vvyādhivivṛddhiñ ca karoti | tam upapādya snehasvedābhyāṃ bhūyo virecayed
                        dṛḍhataraṃ | dṛḍhaṃ pracalitadoṣam vā tṛtīye divasa iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         asnigdhasvinne rūkṣamauṣadham upayuktamabrahmacāriṇā vā vāyuṃ kopayati |
                        tatra vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ pārśvapṛṣṭhaśoṇitamanyāmarmma muśūlaṃ mūrcchā bhrama
                        saṃjñānāśañ ca karoti | tadvātaśūlam ity ācakṣate | tamabhyajya
                        dhānyasvedena svedayitvā yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tailenānu vā vāmayed iti
                        pāṭhaḥ |sayati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehasvedābhyām avibhāvita śarīreṇauṣadhamalpaguṇam vā pītamūrddhamadho vā
                        nābhyeti doṣām̐ścopakleśya taiḥ saha balakṣayamāpādayati | tatrādhmānaṃ
                        hṛdayagrahastṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhaś ca bhavati | tam ayogam ity ācakṣate |tam āśu
                        vāmayed virecayed vā durvvāntasya tu samutkliṣṭā doṣāḥ | vyāpyaśarīraṃ
                        kaṇḍūśvayathukoṭhapiṭakajvarāṅgasādanāni kurvvanti tatas tān aśeṣān
                        sahauṣadhenāpaharet | durvviriktasya tu stabdhapūrṇṇodaratā
                        bastiśūlomeḍhratodo vātamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaśaḥ kaṇḍūrmaṇḍalaprādurbbhāvaś ca
                        bhavati | tamāsthapya punaḥ snehayitvā virecayet tīkṣṇeneti |
                        nātipravarttamāne tiṣṭhati vā duṣṭasaṃśodhane tatsantejanārtham uṣṇodakam
                        pāyayet | pāṇitāpaiś ca pārśvodaram upasvedayet tataḥ pravarttate doṣāḥ |
                        anupravṛtte 'lpe doṣe jīrṇṇecauṣadhe ca bahudoṣam antaḥ śailam balañ
                        cāvekṣya bhūyo mātrāñ ca vidadhyād anupravṛtta bhenyūbhaṃ vā
                        daśajātrādūrddham upasthitadehaṃ bhūyaḥ śodhayed durvviriktamāsthāpya punaḥ
                        snehayitvā virecayet | hrībhayalobhaiś ca vegāghātaśīlāḥ prāyaśaḥstriyo
                        rājasamīpasthā vaṇijaḥ śrotriyāś ca bhavanti | tasmād etair ddurvvirecyāḥ |
                        bahuvātatvāt | ataścaināṃ susvinnasnigdhān virecayed iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnasyātimātramatimṛdukoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇamadhikam vābheṣajamatiyogaṅ
                        kuryāt | tatra vamanātiyoge pittātipravṛttir bbalavisraṃso vātakopo
                        balavām̐ś ca bhavati | tamabhyajyāvagāhya ca śītā svapsu śītaiḥ
                        śarkkarāmiśrair llehair upacared iti | virecanātiyoge
                        kaphātipravṛttiruttarakālañ ca saraktasya tatrāpi balavisraṃsā vātakopo
                        balavām̐ś ca bhavati | tamabhyajya śītābhir adbhiḥ pariṣicyāvagāhya śītais
                        taṇḍulāmbubhir mmadhumiśrair vvāmayet | picchābastiñcāsmai dadyāt |
                        kṣīrarasayoścainam anyatamena bhojayet kṣīrasarppiṣā cainam anuvāsayet |
                        priyaṅgvādiñcāsmai taṇḍulāmbunā pātum prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmin eva ca vamanotiyoge tipravṛtte śoṇitaṃ ṣṭhīvati ccharddayati vā
                        raktaṃ tatra jihvāniḥsaraṇam avasarppaṇañ cākṣṇor vvyāvṛttihanusaṃhananaṃ
                        tṛṣṇā hikkāṅgarau visaṃ jñatvam ity upadravā bhavanti | tam
                        ativisrutaśoṇitavidhānena nopacaret |
                        jihvānniḥsarppitāntrikaṭukalavaṇacūrṇṇapraghṛṣṭāmantaḥ pīḍayet praviṣṭāyām
                        anyemlamasya purastāt khādeyuḥ | vyāvṛtte cākṣiṇī ghṛtābhyaktaiḥ pīḍayet |
                        hanusaṃhanane vātaśleṣmaharan nasyaṃ svedañ ca vidadhyāt | tṛṣṇādiṣu ca
                        yathāsvaṃ pratikurvvīta | visaṃjñam vā veṇuvīṇāgītasv enaṃ srāvayed iti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanātiyoge sacandrakaṃsalilam adhaḥ sravati tato
                        māṃsadhāvanaprakāśamuttarakālaṃ jīvaśoṇitañ ca | tatra gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ
                        vepathur vvamanātiyogopadravāś ca bhavanti | tam atisrutavidhānenaivopacaret
                        | niḥsarppitaṅ gudam abhyajya parisvedyān pīḍayet | kṣudrarogacikitsite
                        gudasraṃsacikitsitañ cāvekṣyeta | vepathau vātavyādhividhānaṅ kurvvīta |
                        jihvāniḥsarppaṇādiṣūktaḥ pratīkāraḥ | atipravṛtte vā nyagrodhādikaṣā
                        yakṣīrekṣurasaghṛtasaṃsṛṣṭaiś cainaṃ bastir upācaret | śoṇitaniṣṭhīvane
                        raktātisāraraktapittakriyāś cānyasya vidadhyān nyagrodhādiñ cāsya
                        pānabhojaneṣūpayuñjīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvaśoṇitaraktapittayo jijñāsārtham picu plotam vātra prakṣipet tad
                        uṣṇodakaprakṣālitam avarajyeta taj jīvaśoṇita m ity avagantavyam amṛgbhoktum
                        vā śune dadyāt sa yady upayuñjyāt taj jīvaśoṇitam ity avagantavyam iti |
                        tayoś ca raktipittātīsārakriyām vidadhīta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa śeṣānnenānilaprāyakoṣṭhenāsnigdhena vā pītamauṣadham ādhmāpayati |
                        tatrānilamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaḥ | samunnaddhodaratā pārśvabhaṅgo gudabastitudanañ
                        ca bhavati | tamādhmānam ity ācakṣate | tam upasvedyānāha
                        varttidīpanabastikriyābhir yojyā iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣāmeṇātimṛdukoṣṭhena tīkṣṇamatyuṣṇam atilavaṇ atirūkṣam vā bheṣajam
                        upayuktam pittānilau pradūṣya nātibastigudaparikarttanam āpādayati | tām
                        parikarttiketyācakṣate || taṃ yaṣṭīmadhukakṛṣṇatilamadhughṛtayuktaiḥ
                        picchābastibhir āsthāpayet | śītāmbupariṣiktañcainaṃ payasā bhuktavantaṃ
                        ghṛtam aṇḍanayaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena vā tailenānuvāsayed iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         krūrakoṣṭhasyātiprabhūtadoṣasya vā mṛdvalpamauṣadhamavacāritaṃ samutkleśya
                        doṣānna niḥśeṣān apaharati | pākañcopaiti | tatra
                        daurbbalyodaraviṣṭambhārucirggātrasadanāni bhavanti | sa vedanau
                        cāsyapittaśleṣmāṇau sravatas tam parisrāvam iti ācakṣate |
                        tamajakarṇṇadhavatiniśa palāsakaṣāyair mmadhuyuktair āsthāpayet |
                        upaśāntadoṣam bhūyaḥ saṃśodhayed</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atirūkṣetisnigdhe vā bheṣajam avacāritam aprāptaṃ purīṣam udīrayato
                        vigevighātena pravāhikā bhavati | tatra sadāha śūlaṃ svetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ raktam vā
                        bhṛśaṃ pravāhamāṇaḥ kapham upaviśati | tam pratisrāvavidhānenopacaret</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yast ūrddhvam adho vā bheṣajaṃ vegapravṛttam ajñānād vinihanti
                        tasyopasaraṇaṃ hṛdi kurvvanti doṣas tatra pradhānamarmmasantāpād vedanābhir
                        atyartham pīḍyamādantāṃ kaṭakaṭāyatyudvṛttākṣo jihvāṃ khādati
                        pratāmyamānacetā ca bhavati | tam abhyajya dhānasvedena svedayitvā tīkṣṇena
                        dviśiro virecanenopacared yaṣṭīmadhukamiśreṇa cainan taṇḍulāmbunā vāmayed
                        yathā doṣaguṇocchreyaś cainam bastibhir upācared iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tūrddhvam adho vā pravṛttadoṣaḥ śītāṅgāram udakam anilam anyad vā
                        seveta tasya doṣāḥ srotaḥsv avalīyamānā ghanībhāvam āpannā
                        vātamūtrapurīṣagraham āpādya vibadhyante || tasyāṭopo jvaro dāho vedanā ca
                        tīvrā bhavati | tam āśu vāmayitvā prāptayitvā prāptakālaṃ kriyāṃ yojayed iti
                        || adho bhāge tv abhāgaharadravye saindhavāmlalavaṇa mūtrasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ pāyayed
                        āsthāpanam anuvāsanañ ca yathādoṣam vidadhyād yathādoṣam āhārakramaś ca |
                        ūrddhvabhāge tu upadravaviśeṣāt yathāsvaṃ pratikurvvīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yā tu virecane gudaparikīrttitā tad vamāne kañcakaṣaṇaṃ yadadhaḥ
                        parisravaṇaṃ sa ūrddhaṅ kaphaprasekaḥ | yā tvadhaḥ pravāhikā sa ūrddhaṅ
                        śuṣkoṅkādgāra iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.34.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yās tv etā vyāpadaḥ proktā daśapañca ca tatvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etā virekāti yogā duryogā yogajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.trailer">|| cikitsā lahya ||</l>
                </div>

                        anekakarmmaprakāratvāt | ba stirihakhalu nānāvidhadravyasaṃyogād doṣāṇāṃ

                        kanīnikānāmikāmadhyamāṅgulipariṇāhāni
                        agreṅgulādhyarddhāṅguladhyarddhāṅgulatryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇṇikāni
                            śyenabarhikaṅkagṛdhrapatranāḍītulya praveśānāni mudgamāṣaka
                        lāyamātrāsrotāṃsi vidadhyān netrāṇīti | teṣu cāsthāpanadravyapramāṇam
                        āturahastasammitausanmiśrau prasṛtau dvau catvārāṣṭau vidheyā |</l>

                        agre tryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇṇikaṃ gṛdhra patranāḍītulyapraveśaṃ
                        kolāsthimātraṃ cchidraṃ klinnakalāyamātracchidram ity eke ||
                        āsthāpanamātrapramāṇaṃ dvādaśaprasṛtā iti | saptasaptyānyās tu
                        ūrddhannetrapramāṇam etad eva | āsthāpanamātrāpramāṇan tu dviraṣṭavarṣavad

                <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 36 (draft based on MS H)</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.36.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto netrabastivyāpaccikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.36.2.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra netrañ calitam vivarttitam pārśvāvapīḍitam atyuttkṣiptam avasannan
                        tiryakkṣiptam iti ṣaghraṇidhānadoṣāḥ | atisthūlaṅ karkkaśāgram avanatam
                        anubhinnasannikṛṣṭakarṇṇikaṃ śūkṣmātimajacchidram alpam atidīrgham
                        atihrasvam ity ekādaśanetradoṣāḥ || bahalatālpatā cchidratā prastdhānatā
                        durbbaladurbbaddheti tveti pañca bastidoṣāḥ | atipīḍitatā śithilapīḍitatā
                        bhūyo vapīḍitatā kālātikramateti catvāraḥ pīḍanadoṣāḥ | āmaṃ hīnam atimātram
                        atiśītam atyuṣṇam atitīkṣṇaṇ ativṛddham atisnigdham atirūkṣm atisāndram
                        atidravam ity ekādaśadravyadoṣāḥ | avāṅcīrṣo cchīrṣony
                        ubjauttānasaṅkucitotthitasatthitādadakṣiṇapārśvaśāyinam avanatapratānam ity
                        aṣṭau śayyādoṣāḥ | evam etāḥ pañcacatvāriṃśad vyāpado vaidyanimattā bhavanti
                        |āturanimittās tu pañcadaśa āturopadravīye vakṣyante | snehastvaṣṭābhiḥ
                        kāraṇaiḥ praṇihito na pratyāgacchati | tad yathā tribhir doṣai
                        rasanābhibhūto malavyāmiśro dūrānupraviṣṭo svinnasyānuṣṇolpaṃ bhuktavato
                        lpāṃśaś cetyetāḥ | vaidyāturanimittā bhavanti | ubhayor bbastyor ayogaḥ |
                        ādhmānaṃ parikarttaḥ parisrāvaḥpravāhikā hṛdayopasaraṇam aṅgapragraho tiyogo
                        jīvādānam ity etān avavyāpado vaidyanimittā eva bhavanti || ṣaṭsaptabhiḥ
                        samāsena vyāpadaḥ parikīrttitāḥ |tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vijñānaṃ siddhiñ ca
                        tadanantaraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.36.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         netre vicalite cāpi varttite gudaveṣṭanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rukkṣatam vā bhavet tatra vidhiḥ pittakṣatāpahaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.36.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atyutkṣipte 'vasanne ca netre pāyau ca vedanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavatyatrāpi pittaghno vidhiḥ snehaiś ca sevanaṃ ||</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         pāyau tato rukkṣatañ ca siddhis tatrāpi pūrvavat ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.7">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.37.124</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bastau dahyati vā bāḍhaṃ pāyau bastim pradāpayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.125">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.37.125</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śukran duṣṭaṃ śoṇitañcāṅganānām asṛgdarantasya nāśañ ca kaṣṭaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūtrāghātam mūtradoṣān pravṛddhān yonau rogān aparāyāś ca saṅgāṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.126">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.37.126</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śukrāghātaṃ śarkkarām aśmarīñ ca śukraṃ bastau vaṃkṣaṇe mehane ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         ghorān anyān bastijām̐ś cāpirogān mehodṛte tūttarau hanti bastiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.127">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.37.127</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag dattasya vijñānam vyāpadaḥ krama eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         baster uttarasaṃjñasya samānaṃ snehabastineti || o ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">cikitsālañ ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="38" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 38 (draft based on MS H)</head>





                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto nirūhakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38a">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarirddharmmabhṛtām variṣṭham amṛtodbhavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraṇāvupasaṃṅgṛhya suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38b">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagavaṃ snehavastes tu tathaivāsthāpanasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pramāṇaṅkalpanaṅ kālam mātrāñ cāpi bravīhi me ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38c">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38c</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhe muhūrtte karaṇe dine ca nakṣatrayoge ca tathānukūle |
                        <caesura/>
                         viviktasaṃsṛṣṭamṛdāvalipte vicitrapuṣpāstṛtabhūpradeśe ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38d">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38d</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         suvarṇṇarūpyāya satāmrajo vā mṛdūdbhavo vā kalaśo 'mbupūrṇṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadhānyaratnādi samālyagandhair vastrādibhiś cāpy atha svastikaiś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38e">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38e</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taccāmṛtasthānam ato 'rccanīyaṃ pūrvvāt tatonyaddhṛṣayaḥ sadevāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃspṛśya ratnāni tathauṣadhīm̐ś ca devān dvijān pūjya ca dakṣiṇābhiḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38f">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38f</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravāṇi sarvvāṇi tu vāmapārśve cūrṇṇāni kalkān atha dakṣiṇe tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         tanmadhya saṃsthāyabhiṣak prasanna iti pāṭhaḥ |bhiṣag apramattaḥ sunirmmale
                        syāt sudṛḍho viśāle ||
                        <caesura/>
                         suvarṇṇalohādi mṛdūdbhavo vā pragṛhyakāṃse 'py atha rājate vā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38g">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38g</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         datvād au saindhavasyākṣaṃ madhunaḥ prasṛtam mitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pātre talena mathnīyāt tadvat snehaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38h">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38h</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gūḍhasneham viditvā tu vinītaḥ kalkamāvapet |
                        <caesura/>
                         datvā samyak sumathite phalakalkamataḥ paraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38i">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38i</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato yathocitāñ ceṣān kārṣikān ślakṣṇapeṣimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         gambhīre bhojane nyasya khajenābhimathet tataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38j">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38j</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ca sādhu manyeta na sāndro na tanuḥ samaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyaḥ prasṛtāt pañca supūrṇṇāt tatra dāpayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38k">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38k</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasakṣīrāmlamūtrāṇān doṣāvasthām avekṣya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         evam añjalayaḥ ṣaḍtaiḥ kuryād vyādhitapāṇinā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38l">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38l</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dvādaśaprasṛtaṃ kecid viṅśatiḥ palikan tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dvātriṅśat palikāṃś caiva triṃśad aṣṭau tathaiva ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         evam bhinneṣu śāstreṣu saṃśayaḥ sumahānabhūt || o ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āturam anuvāsitam āsthāpayet | svabhyaktaṃ svinnaśarīram utsṛṣṭa
                        bahirbbhāgamapravāte śucau deśe samavinyastāyāṃ śayyāyām adhaḥ |
                        sapratigrahāyām āśroṇīpradeśe suvyūhāyāṃ śayānam vāmapārśve neti || bhavati
                        cātra ślokaḥ || savyam prasārayet sakthi dakṣiṇaṃ cāpasaṃharet | madhyāhne
                        sumanājīrṇṇe niranno vāgyatonaraḥyataḥ || tato vāmapādopari netraṃ
                        kṛtvetarapādāṅguṣṭhāṅgulībhyāṅ karṇṇikopari nipīḍya bastāv
                        auṣadhamāsicyocchrāsyauṣadhānte cāvavadhya mūtreṇa samyag baddhañ cāturā ya
                        ghṛtābhyaktanetrāgraṃ ghṛtābhyakta gudāya praṇayed anutsṛjannanupṛṣṭhavaṃśam
                        anusukham ākarṇṇikam iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bastiṃ savye kare kṛtvā dakṣiṇena avapīḍayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         ekenaiva ca pīḍena na drutan na vilambitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato netram apanīya triṃśan mātrāpīḍanakālād upetyottiṣṭhetyāturam brūyāt |
                        utkuṭukobhavatasterāgamanāyeti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anena vidhinā dadyād bastiṃ bastiviśāradaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dvitīyam vā tṛtīyam vā caturtham vā yathārthataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaṅ nirūḍhaliṅge tu prāptabastin nivārayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         api hīnaṃ kramaṅ kuryān na ca kuryād atikramaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣāt sukumārāṇāṃ hīna eva kramo hitaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         alpālpavego vinvāta hīnohīno nirūhaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         yasya mūtrapurīṣañ ca kaphavāyuś ca gacchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         krameṇa laghutā caiva sunirūhaḥ samānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sunirūḍhantato jantuṃ snātaṃ bhuktarasodanaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8.3">

                        <caesura/>
                         yathoktena vidhānena yojayet snehabastinā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.38.8.4</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         paś cādagnibalam matvā pavanasya ca veṣṭitaṃ ||</l>

                         balātelaina deyāḥ syur bbastayas traivṛtena vā || o ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.89.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāta āturopadravakitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehapīsya vāntasya viriktasyāśrutāsṛjaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nirūḍhasya ca kāyāgnir mando bhavati dehinaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         so nnair atyarthagurubhir upayuktaiḥ praśāmyati |
                        <caesura/>
                         alpo mahadbhir bahudhā chādite gnir ivendhanaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa cālpair laghubhiś cānnair upayuktair vivardhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāṣṭhair aṇubhir alpaiś ca sandhukṣita ivānalaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtadoṣapramāṇena sa cāhāravidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         trīṇi cātra pramāṇāni prastho rdhāḍhakam āḍhakam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāvaraṃ prasthamātraṃ dve śeṣe madhyamottame |
                        <caesura/>
                         prasthe tv eke gate deyā yavāgūsvalpatāṇḍulā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dve caivārdhāḍhake deye tisraś cāpy āḍhake gate |
                        <caesura/>
                         vilepīmucitādbhaktāc caturthāṃśakṛtām bhiṣak | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.9"> dadyāt klinnan tataḥ paścāt mudgayūṣeṇa bhojanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tribhāgakalitaṃ samyag akṛtenārddhasammitaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.10a"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.12">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.22">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.25">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.26">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guhyapradeśe śvayathuṃ kāśaśvāsau ca dāruṇau |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.28</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
