                        <caesura/>
                         tamasā cābhibhūtaś ca svapnam evābhinandati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         uccaiḥ sambhāṣaṇād vāyuḥ śirasy āpādayed rujaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āndhyam vādhiryamaghratvaṃ mūkatā jaḍatām api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31a">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.31a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         arditaṃ sahanum mokṣam adhīmantha dāruṇaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.31b"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         labhate dantacālañ ca tāṃs tāṃś cānyān upadravān |
                        <caesura/>
                         yānayānāt tu labhate cchardiṃ mūrcchā bhramaṃ klamaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāṅgapragrahaṃ ghoram indriyāṇāñ ca vibhramaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāsanāt tathā sthānāc chroṇyāṃ bhavati vedanā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aticaṅkramaṇād vāyur jaṃghorvvoḥ kurute rujaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakthnoḥ praśoṣaṃ śopham vā pādaharṣam athāpi vā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35a">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.35a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītasambhogatoyānāṃ sevā mārutavṛddhaye |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.35b"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātātapābhyām vaivarṇyaṃ jvaraṃ vāpi nigacchati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         viruddhādhyaśanān mṛtyuṃ vyādhiṃ vā ghoram arcchati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         asātmyabhojanād dhanyād balavarṇṇāvasaṃśayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anātmavantaḥ paśuvad bhuñjate ye pramāṇataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rogānīkasya te mūlam ajīrṇṇāt prāpnuvanti haḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāpadāṃ kāraṇaṃ vīkṣya vyāpatsv eteṣu buddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         prayatetāturārogyai pratyanīkena hetunā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.39.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viriktavāntair hariṇaiṇalāvakāḥ śaśāś ca sevyāḥ samayūratittirāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṣaṣṭikāś cāpi purāṇaśālayas tathaiva mudgā laghu yac ca kīrttitam iti
                        ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer"> || ci 39 || ❈ || </p>





                </div>


                <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 40]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dhūmanastaḥ kavalacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcavidho dhūmo bhavati | tad yathā | prāyogikaḥ snaihiko vairecanikaḥ
                        kāsaghno vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrailādinā kuṣṭhatagaravarjyena ślakṣṇapiṣṭena dvādaśāṅgulaṃ śarakāṇḍaṃ
                        daśāṅgulagarbham aṅgula m aṅguṣṭhodara pariṇāhaṃ kṣaumeṇāṣṭāṅgulam
                        pariveṣṭyālepayed eṣā varttiḥ prāyogikaḥ ||
                        snehaphalasāramadhūcchiṣṭasarjarasagugguluprabhṛtibhiś ca snehamiśraiḥ
                        snaihikaiḥ || śirovirecanadravyair vairecanikaiḥ ||
                        bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikātrikaṭukakāsamardahiṃgviṅgudītvaṅmanaḥśilācchinnaruhākarkaṭakasṛṅgīprabhṛtibhiḥ
                        kāsaharaiḥ kāsaghnaiḥ |
                        snāyucarmakhuraśṛṅgakarkaṭāsthiśuṣkamatsyavallūrakrimibhir vāmanīyaiś ca
                        vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra bastinetravyavyair dūmanetradravyāni vyākhyātāni bhavanti ||
                        dhūmanetraṃ tu kanīnikāpariṇāham agre kalāyamātrasroto mūle ṅguṣṭhapariṇāhaṃ
                        dhūmavarttipraveśasroto ṅgulāni catuścatvāriṃśat prāyogike | dvātriṃśat
                        snaihike | caturviṃśati vairecanike | ṣoḍaśakāsaghne | daśa vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha sukhopaviṣṭaḥ sumanā ṛjvadhodṛṣṭir atandritaḥ | snehapradīptāgrām
                        varttinetrasrotasi praṇidhāya dhūmam pibed iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhena tam pibet pūrvaṃ nāsikābhyān tataḥ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhapītaṃ mukhenaiva vamet pītañ ca nas tataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo vamen nastato dhūman nastapītaṃ mukhena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa netrakarṇṇanāsāsyasaṃśrayāl labhate gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu prāyogikaṃ ghrāṇenādadyāt | snaihikaṃ mukhanāsābhyāṃ |
                        nāsikābhyāṃ vairecanikaṃ | mukhenaivetarāv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        śramabhayāmarṣoṣṇaviṣaraktapittamadamūrcchāpipāsātāluśoṣamūrdhābhighātodgāratimiramehodarādhmānordhvavātontravṛddhibālavṛddhadurbalaviraktāsthāpitajāgaritagarbhiṇīrūkṣakṣatakṣīṇoraskāḥ
                        madhughṛtadadhidugdhamadyayavāgūpītāḥ svalpakaphāś ca dhūman na severann iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         akālapīto bhramarī śirorogaṃ karoti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāsrotokṣijihvānāṃm upaghātañ ca dāruṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmaḥ snaihiko vairecanikaḥ prāyogiko dvādaśasu kāleṣūpayogo bhavati ||
                        tad yathā
                        kṣutadantaprakṣālananasyasnānabhojanādivāsvapnamaithunacchardanamūtroccārābhir
                        uṣitaśastrakarmānteṣv iti || tasya vibhāgo
                        mūtroccārakṣavathuruṣitamaithunānteṣu snaihikaḥ | divāsvapnacchardanāntayor
                        vairecanikaḥ | dantaprakṣālanasya snānabhojanaśastrakarmānteṣu prāyogika iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra snaihiko vātaṃ śamayati | snehād upalepitvāc ca | vairecanikaḥ
                        śleṣmāṇam utkliśyāpakarṣati raukṣyāt taikṣṇyād auṣṇyād vaiṣadyāc ca |
                        prāyogikaḥ śleṣmāṇam utkleśayaty utkliṣṭaṃ cāpakarṣayati śamayati vā
                        sādhāraṇatvāt pūrvābhyām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmaprayogāt puruṣaḥ prasannendriyavāṅmanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛḍhakeśadvijaḥ śmaśrusugandhiviśadānanaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā
                        kāsaśvāsārocakāsyapralepasvarabhedamukhāsrāvakṣavathuvamathukrāthatandrīhanumanyāstambhapīnasaśirorogalocanaśūlāvātakaphanimittāś
                        cāsya mukharogā na bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya yogāyogātiyogā vijñātavyā bhavanti | yogas tu dṛṣṭaphalārthaḥ | ayogo
                        rogānirjayaḥ | atiyogas
                        tāluśoṣaparidāhapipāsābhramamadamūrcchākarṇṇakṣveladṛṣṭirogādaurbalyayutam
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra prāyogikas trīṃs trīn ucchvāsān ādadyāt paryāgatāns trīns trīṃś
                        caturo veti || snaihikaṃ yāvad asrupravṛttiḥ || vairecanikam ādoṣadarśanāt
                        || grāsāntareṣu kāsaharaṃ || vairecanikavat tilataṇḍulayavāgūpīto vāmanīyaṃ
                        yathāyoga iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vraṇabastinetreṇa vraṇadhūmanetraṃ vyākhyātam bhavati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śarāvasampuṭayutaṃ vraṇadhūman nayed vraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmanetreṇa matimān vedanāsrāvaśāntaye ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhir eṣa samāsena dhūmasyābhihito mayā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ kuśalasammitaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         auṣadhapakvo vā sneho nāsikābhyāṃ pradīyate | nasyan tatpañcavikalpam
                        bhavati | tad yathā | nasyaṃ śirovirecanaṃ pratimarśo vapīḍaḥ pradhamanam
                        iti | teṣān nasyam pradhāṇaṃ śirovirecanaṃ yena nasya vikalpaḥ pratimarśaḥ |
                        śirovirecanavikalpo vapīḍaḥ pradhamanañ ceti | tato nastaśabdaḥ pañcavidhā
                        ṇipatati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra yaḥ snehārthaṃ śūnyaśirasāṃ grīvāskandhorasāṃ balajananārthaṃ
                        dṛṣṭiprasādajananārtham vā sneha upādīyate tasmin vaiśeṣike nastaśabdaḥ |
                        tat tu deyam vātābhipanne śirasi tathā
                        dantakeśaśmasruṇātadāruṇakarṇṇakṣvelatimirasvaropaghātanāsārogamukharogaśoṣāvabāhukākālajavalīpalitaprabodheṣu
                        vātapaittikeṣu ca mukharogeṣu vātapittaharadravyasiddhena sneheneti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanam api śleṣmaṇābhivyāptatālugataśirasāṃ tathā
                        rocakaśirogauravaśūlapīnasāvabhedakakrimipratiśyāyāpasmāraghrāṇājñāneṣv
                        anyeṣu cordhvajatrugateṣu vikāreṣu śirovirecanadravyasiddhena sneheneti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tat tv etad dvividham apy uktaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatroccāritavātamūtrapurīṣāya bhuktavate vyabhre kāle
                        pāṇitāpopasveditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśāya vātātaparajohīne veśmany
                        uttānaśāyine kiñcit pravilambitaśirase vastrāvacchāditanetrāya
                        vāmahastapradeśinyagronnāmitanāsāgrāya viśuddhasrotase dakṣiṇahastena śuktyā
                        picunā vā sukhoṣṇam adrutam avicchinnadhārām āsiñced iti | yathā ca netreṇa
                        prāpnoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehe vasicyati śiro na kathañ cana kampayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhāṣen na ca kupyec ca na kṣuyān na hased api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.27">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etair hi vihataḥ sneho na samyak pratipadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kāsaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ śirokṣigadasambhavaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya pramāṇan tv aṣṭau bindavaḥ pradeśinīparvadvayaniḥsrutāḥ | eṣā mātrā
                        prathamā | dvitīyā śuktiḥ tṛtīyā pāṇiśuktir ity etās tisro mānāḥ yathābalam
                        prayojyā bhavantīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.29"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛṅgāṭakam abhiplāvya nireti vadanād yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphotkleśabhayāccainan niṣṭhīved avidhārayan || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.31">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dante punar api saṃsvedya galakapolādīn dhūmam āseveta | bhojayec cainam
                        anabhiṣyanti | athāsyācārikam upadiśet | krodhādim pariharec ca |
                        rajodhūmamanastāpadravapānaśirasnānādīni | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.32">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya yogāyogātiyogavijñānaṃ bhavati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.33">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lāghavaṃ śiraso yoge sukhasvapnaprabodhaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vikāropaśamaḥ śuddhir indriyāṇām paraṃ sukhaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.34">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ayoge rogānirjayaḥ kaphaprasekaḥ śiraso gurutendriyavibhramaḥ | k> atiyoge
                        tāluśoṣapipāsābhramamadamūrcchā ceti lakṣaṇam mūrdhny atisnigdhe rūkṣaṃ
                        tatrāvacārayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.35"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.36">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanasyāpi catvāro bindavaḥ ṣaḍ vā tathāṣṭau vā yathābalam
                        śirovicakasnehasya pramāṇam abhinirdiśet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.37">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya trīṇy abhivarṇṇyante lakṣaṇāni prayogataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhihīnātisañjñāni viśeṣāc chāstracintakaiḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.38">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lāghavaṃ śirasaḥ śuddhiḥ srotasāṃ vyādhinirjayaḥ | cittendriyaprasādaś ca
                        śirasaḥ śuddhilakṣaṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.39">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṇḍūpade gurutā srotasāṃ kaphasambhavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnāviśuddhe śirasi lakṣaṇam parikīrttitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.40">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mastuluṅgāgamo vā tad dṛṣṭir indriyavibhramaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śūnyatā śirasaś cāpi mūrdhni gāḍhavirecite || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.41">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hīnātiśuddhe śirasi kaphavātaghnam ācaret |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag virecite cāpi sarpir naste nuṣecayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.42">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nasye tu parirharttavyā bhavanti | tad yathā </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.43"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.45"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.47">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhuktavān apatarpitotyarthaṃ taruṇapratiśyāyī garbhinī madyadravapīḍito
                        jīrṇṇīvastidantaḥ kruddho rāgārttaḥ tṛṣṇābhibhūto bālo vṛddhaḥ śrānto
                        vegāvarodharataḥ śirasnātukāmaś ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.48"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.49">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nasye śirovireke ca vyāpado dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣotkleśakṣayāc caiva vijñeyā ca yathākramaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.50">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.50</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrotkleśanimittāsu yuñjyāc chamanaśodhaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         atha kṣayanimittāsu yathāsvaṃ bṛṃhaṇaṃ hitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.51">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.51</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratimarśes tu caturdaśasu kāleṣūpadeyo bhavati | tad yathā | kālyotthitena
                        | prakṣālitadantena | gṛhān nirgacchatā | vyāyāmavyavāyapariśrātena |
                        mūtroccārakavalāñjanān te bhuktavatā | charditavatā | divāsvapnotthitena
                        sāyañ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.52">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.52</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra kālyotthitenāsevitaḥ pratimarśo rātrāv upacitaṃ nāsāsrotogataṃ malam
                        apahanti | prakṣālitadantena dantānāṃ dṛḍhatā vadanasaugandhyañ cāpādayati |
                        gṛhān nirgacchatā nāsāsrotaso snehaklinnatayā | rajodhūmo vā na prabādhate |
                        vyāyāmavyavāyapariśrāntena śramam apahanti | mūtroccārānte dṛṣṭigurutvam
                        apanayati | kavalāñjanānte dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayati | bhuktavatā sroto viśuddhiṃ
                        laghutvaṃ cāpādayati | charditavatā srotovilagnaṃ śleṣmāṇam apohya
                        bhaktacchaṃdaṃ kurute | divāsvapnotthitena nidrāśeṣaṃ gauravañ cāpahatya
                        cittaikāgryaṃ janayati | sāyaṃ sukhanidrāprabodham āpādayatīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.53">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.53</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         īṣad ucchiṃghaṇāt sneho yadā vaktum prapadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         naste niśiktaṃ taṃ vidyāt pratimarśaṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.54">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.54</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tena rogāḥ praśāmyanti narāṇām ūrdhvajatrujāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         indriyāṇāñ ca vaimalyaṃ kuryād āsyasugandhi ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.55">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.55</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hanudantaśirogrīvātrikabāhūrasāṃ balaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         valīpalitakhālityavyaṃgānāñ cāpy asambhavaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.56">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.56</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tailaṃ kaphe ca vāte ca kevalaṃ pavane vasāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dadyān nastaḥ sadā pitte sarpirmajjāsamārute || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.57">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.57</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvidhasya snehasya vidhir eṣa prakīrttitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmasthānāvirodhitvāt teṣu tailaṃ viśiṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avapīḍan tu śirovirecanavad abhiṣyaṇṇasarpadaṣṭamūrcchitavisaṃjñebhyo
                        dadyāc chirovirecanadravyāṇām anyatamam āsādyāvapīḍam iṣyateti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.46">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cetovikārakrimiviṣād iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.44a">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.44a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarkarekṣurasakṣīrā ghṛtamāṃsarasāṃ pṛthak kṣīṇānāṃ nastato dadyādd
                        raktapittagadeṣu ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.58">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.58</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ataḥ param pravakṣyāmi kavaḍagrahaṇe vidhiṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturdhā kavaḍasnehī prasādī śodhiropaṇau | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.59">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.59</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sngidhoṣṇaiḥ snaihiko vāte svāduśītaiḥ prasādanaḥ pitte kaṭvamblalavaṇai
                        rūkṣaiḥ saṃśodhaṇaḥ kaphe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.60">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.60</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyatiktamadhuraiḥ kaṭūṣṇo ropaṇo vraṇe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.61">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.61</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra trikaṭukāśitasarṣapasiddhārthakakalkam āloḍya
                        tailamūtrakṣārasurāśuktamadhūnām anyatamena salavaṇam abhiprataptam
                        upasvinnamṛditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśe dhārayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.62">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.62</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaṃ sañcāryate yā tu mātrā sā kavalaḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         asañcāryā tu yā mātrā gaṇḍūṣaḥ sā prakīrttitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.63">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.63</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tāvac ca dhārayitavyo nanyamanasānunnatadehena yāvad
                        doṣapratipūrṇṇagalakapolatvaṃ nāsāsrotonayanapariplavaś ca bhavati tadā
                        vimoktavyaḥ | punaś cānyo grahītavyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.64">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.64</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evaṃ snehapayaḥkṣaudrarasamūtrāmblasambhṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kasāyoṣṇodakābhyāñ ca kavaḍā doṣato hitāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.65">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.65</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādher apacayas tuṣṭir viṣadaṃ vaktralāghavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         indriyāṇām prasādaś ca kavaḍe śuddhilakṣaṇaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.66">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.66</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hīne jāḍyakaphotkleśā varasajñānam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         atiyogāt mukhe pākaḥ śoṣas tṛṣṇāruciklamaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.67">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.67</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanīye viśeṣeṇa bhavaty etat tu lakṣaṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tilāṃ nīlotpalaṃ sarpiḥ śarkarā kṣīram eva ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.68">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.68</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sakṣaudro dagdhavarktrasya gaṇḍūṣo dāhanāśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kavalasya samāsena vidhir eṣaḥ prakīrttitaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.69">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.69</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vibhajya bheṣajaṃ budhyā kurvīta pratisāraṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kalko rasakriyā kṣaudraṃ cūrṇṇañ ceti caturvidhaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.70">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.70</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṅgulyagrapraṇītan tu yathāsvam mukharogiṇāṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya yogam ayogañ ca kavaloktaṃ vibhāvayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.71">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.71</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhojayet cānabhiṣyandi doṣaghnam aśanaṃ naram iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.trailer"> || ci 40 || 0 || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.72">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.72</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sneha svedo vamanaṃ virekaṃ vyāpadaṃ tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         netre pramāṇa vyāpac cānuvāsanasahottaraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.73">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.73</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nirūhottarapīḍā ca dhūmanastena vai daśa || ❈ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.74">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1938 ed., 4.40.74</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yad uktañ catvāriṃśac cikitsitānīti tat sarvaṃ samāptam iti || ❈ ||</l>
